Current Affairs Commentary

The Crisis After the Fall of Rehe 14

Following the loss of half of the country in Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, and just when the people of the entire country were anxiously waiting and hoping, a sudden thunderbolt struck, and Rehe was declared to have fallen again.

Indeed, the fall of Rehe was already expected by us. After all, with Tang Yulin, who only knew how to levy exorbitant taxes and squeeze the lifeblood of the people, saying that he could fight to the death against Japan was something we dared not believe. Moreover, this lonely city with its setting sun and dying embers, under the fierce firepower and heavy troop attacks of the Japanese, would ultimately be unable to withstand this dangerous situation, which was also an inevitable result in fact. However, we believe that Rehe's mountainous terrain is a natural defense. If our army could have even a fraction of the determination to resist, the enemy would not have been able to drive straight in. At the same time, since the situation in Rehe became critical, the military authorities in North China repeatedly expressed their determination to defend Rehe to the death. Military bonds for defending Rehe and resisting Japan have also been issued. Perhaps with considerable resistance, the situation of confrontation could have been extended for at least several months. Even if Rehe could not ultimately avoid falling, the Japanese would have had to pay a huge price. However, today, it has been only ten days since the Japanese army officially launched its invasion of Rehe, and Chengde has already been lost. In a mountainous terrain with natural defenses, the Japanese army has been able to enter as if there were no people. The Chinese army on the front lines of Rehe has been acting as a guide for the Japanese army. Otherwise, no matter what, the fall of Rehe would not have been so rapid.

Rehe has already fallen. According to a telegram from Beiping, Zhang Xueliang expressed indignation, severely reprimanded the righteous army for not firing a single shot, ordered them not to retreat, and issued an arrest warrant for Tang Yulin, who abandoned the city and fled. This kind of severe measure is something we strongly endorse. However, since the September 18th Incident, the government has never punished the generals who abandoned their posts, lost territory, and retreated at the sight of the enemy. Tang Yulin's abandonment of the city and flight is therefore not an isolated incident. Tang Yulin's crime deserves death, but is Tang Yulin the only one whose crime deserves death? Who abandoned the Northeast? Who abandoned Jinzhou? Who abandoned Yuguan? Only with the main generals who did not resist could Tang Yulin dare to abandon the city and flee. Only with no punishment for those who abandoned the city could Tang Yulin dare to have no reservations. Now Rehe is lost. Tang Yulin has fled. The people of the entire country look north with grief and indignation, already feeling that they have no tears to shed. If only one Tang Yulin is arrested, how can the grief and indignation of the people of the entire country be alleviated?

The loss of Rehe was not due to the Japanese army's attack, but to our country's consistent policy of [not striving for national survival]. Perhaps some short-sighted people believe that with the loss of Rehe, the Japanese have achieved their goal, and from now on, both sides can live in peace and without incident. This can be seen from the fact that government bonds have risen instead of falling. However, they do not know that the crisis facing our country after the fall of Rehe is becoming more and more serious. First, with the removal of the barrier to North China, Beiping and Tianjin have no defenses to rely on, and North China will be under Japanese control at all times. Second, with the fall of Rehe, the supply route for the Northeast Volunteer Army has been cut off, and the hopes of the 30 million people of the Northeast for the government to recover the lost territory have also vanished. Third, due to the stimulation of the Rehe Incident, North China may form a confrontation between [resistance] and [non-resistance], giving the Japanese an excuse to advance further. Fourth, how to settle the troops retreating from Rehe, and the issue of public security, are also extremely worrying. In short, after the fall of the three northeastern provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, there is still the fall of Rehe. After the non-resistance of the September 18th Incident, there is still the non-resistance of Rehe. We say every day that we will share the national crisis together, but the result of sharing the national crisis is like this. Our nation has no way to explain itself to the world, and our military authorities have no way to explain themselves to the people of the entire country.

Inaugural Address of the Thirty-Second President of the United States, Franklin D. Roosevelt 15

Externally...Maintain the Dignity of Treaties and Seek to Restore World Trade Prosperity

Internally...Strive to Stabilize Financial Panic and Relieve Rural Distress

(Washington) President Roosevelt's long-awaited inaugural address was mainly focused on domestic affairs, discussing in detail the stabilization of finances, the restoration of normalcy, worker unemployment, and rural distress, in order to address the various thorny issues currently facing the new government. As for foreign policy and international issues, there were only a few words, the main points of which were roughly as follows: "The international trade relations of our United States are important, but at this time, they are secondary to establishing a solid national policy. I will do my best to seek to restore world trade through international economic adjustments, but the urgent domestic situation today cannot wait for this to be achieved first. As for the position of world policy, I am willing to offer this country to the policy of good neighborliness. Anyone who is determined to respect their own rights and the rights of others, and who respects their treaty obligations and sanctity, is our good neighbor," etc. As for Roosevelt's speech on domestic affairs, the main points were roughly as follows: "In a great country, we will be able to respond to these difficulties and return to the realm of prosperity. Therefore, we must first embrace a firm belief. The only thing we have to fear at this time is nameless, unreasonable, and unwarranted fear. This fear alone is enough to discourage people and turn progress into retreat. I firmly believe that you will support your leader in times of difficulty. With this spirit of mine and yours, we can undoubtedly cope with the common difficulties." Roosevelt then explained the country's current difficulties and the bright future ahead, and criticized the shortcomings of the American banking system. Then, he summarized the two ways to restore prosperity, stating: "Today's most urgent task is to provide people with work. This can be accomplished by the government dealing with the economic situation as if dealing with a wartime emergency, requisitioning resources to achieve a part of this. He believes that the government's plan to encourage the development of natural resources is not enough, and private individuals should also make great efforts in this regard. Although this problem is complex and difficult, he will lead the country to solve it." He also said that "some people must recognize that people are too concentrated in industrial hubs and should strive to make good use of the land and increase agricultural product prices. This will increase people's purchasing power. This plan will also prevent congestion losses and will be assisted by the federal, state, and local governments to reduce costs. If the state plans to supervise all transportation, communication, and public utilities, it can prevent unnecessary losses and save huge amounts of waste. Furthermore, all banks and lending and investment institutions must be strictly supervised to prevent the bad habit of using other people's money for speculative purposes. In addition, there must be a suitable and stable currency. These are all urgent tasks at present. He will prepare a special message outlining the plan to implement these plans and send it to Congress for its adoption." Finally, Roosevelt asked the entire country to abide by discipline and sacrifice for the public good. He guaranteed that he would serve as the leader of the people under this guarantee. He is prepared to follow his constitutional responsibilities and propose these plans to the Congress that is about to convene and ask them to quickly adopt them together with other plans that Congress proposes. But if this approach cannot be adopted by Congress and the state of affairs is still extremely critical, then he will ask Congress to give him the most powerful tools to deal with the emergency situation, expanding executive power to the extent that the president has during an invasion by a foreign enemy, so as to combat the emergency situation. (4th National News Agency Dispatch) The Ceremony Was Extremely Bizarre and Colorful

Elephants, Wine Barrels, and Wooden Horses

Everything Was Available

The American Financial Crisis Intensifies 16

Banks in Forty-Eight States All Engulfed in Vortex, Limiting Withdrawals

New Government Assembles National Strength to Plan Rescue Measures

(Special Session of Congress to be Called Within Days)

(Washington) The American financial crisis is intensifying. By sunset today, banks in all forty-eight states had fully implemented restrictions on withdrawals. Bankers from major cities are rushing to the capital to assist the government in jointly devising measures to restore normalcy. President Roosevelt has scheduled a meeting with Congressional leaders on Sunday to finalize the date for a special session of Congress. It is expected that the order for the session will be issued immediately after the decision is made, and Congress may convene as early as Tuesday. Even before the inauguration ceremony was completed, after the new President had just returned to the White House from the Capitol, party leaders were already conferring on the bills the President would propose. The President is currently preparing a special message to be sent to the new Congress, summarizing these bills. However, solutions to remedy the current situation have yet to be finalized late into the night. Bankers and officials are gathering proposals from all sides, selecting the most timely ones to compile into bills. As soon as the inauguration ceremony was completed, the new President began to address the economic problems. In addition to deciding to meet with members of Congress on Sunday, he also instructed Treasury Secretary Woodin to discuss relief measures with national bankers. He also agreed to personally meet with banking and financial experts from Philadelphia and New York on Sunday, and ordered all national postal savings banks to remain open for business as usual until further notice. Roosevelt has now begun to assemble the strength of national bankers to help quell the crisis, and is compiling detailed charts of the measures taken by various states to prevent bank runs and stabilize public confidence. He is also collecting reports from clearinghouse committees and bank resolutions from various regions for research and reference. The New York Clearing House Association has decided to issue small-denomination scrip to replace currency, jointly guaranteed by New York banks for commercial transactions. The Philadelphia Clearing House Association has suggested that Pennsylvania banks extend the moratorium for another week until satisfactory regulations are enacted. Furthermore, Philadelphia bankers have also suggested a ban on gold exports. Political circles here were alarmed upon hearing this news and inquired with the Treasury Department. However, the Treasury Department has not made a formal statement, only indicating that Woodin will discuss the matter after the bankers arrive in the capital in the next day or two. It is reported that at dawn today, only half of the forty-eight states had implemented restrictions. Upon hearing that banks in New York and Illinois had suspended operations, one state after another followed suit. By noon, when the President was inaugurated, most states had been engulfed in the vortex. Indiana and South Carolina were the last states to restrict withdrawals. However, in places like Enid, Oklahoma, the National Guard was mobilized to force banks to comply with the moratorium order. Even though the local banks had sufficient cash on hand, the authorities ordered them to suspend operations to maintain uniformity. Many financiers believe that this concerted action is beneficial to resolving the crisis, as it can put all parts of the country in equilibrium, making it easier to reach a consensus on favorable Congressional solutions. In places like Chautauqua, New York, after hearing the news that the state was also implementing restrictions, state troops were mobilized to protect banks to prevent accidents. However, depositors were able to remain calm upon hearing the news. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

First Meeting of the New Cabinet 17

(Washington) After the swearing-in ceremony, the new cabinet held a temporary meeting. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt is scheduled to convene leaders of the Democratic Party in Congress tomorrow to jointly decide on the date of the special session. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Unemployed Workers March and Demonstrate 18

(Washington) After President Roosevelt's inaugural address was broadcast nationwide via radio, Roosevelt shook hands with people near the podium and then rode in a car to inspect the parade. The crowd cheered along the way. The parade then began to pass in front of the viewing platform. However, there were incidents of demonstrations and disturbances by Communist Party members and unemployed workers in various parts of the United States today. In Detroit, the Communist Party gathered people to march on the main streets, demanding immediate payment of small bank deposits. In Chicago, Communist Party members and unemployed workers also stormed into the City Council, demanding relief money and food, but there were no riots. The situation in Pittsburgh was more serious, with police clashing with Communist Party members in the city, resulting in sixteen arrests. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

There was no wave of withdrawals. As for the proposal to ban gold exports, it is rumored that it is also accompanied by a suggestion to have the federal government guarantee bank deposits nationwide. (National Telegram, 4th)

Ban on Gold Exports Gains Momentum 19

(Washington) The talk of banning gold exports is rampant today. Financial experts say that it is indeed possible for the US government to ban cash from leaving the country on the one hand and allow people to freely exchange cash for currency on the other. As for the amount of currency in circulation, there is currently a reserve of 400 million gold dollars in the treasury as a backing. Therefore, banning gold exports only guarantees that the treasury's gold reserves will not flow out. (National Telegram, 4th)

All of Europe Temporarily Suspends Foreign Exchange with the US 20

(London) In practice, all of Europe has temporarily suspended US dollar transactions. Banks everywhere are refusing to honor US dollar drafts or letters of credit. Lloyd's here has underwritten insurance against losses in the event that the United States abandons the gold standard, with a term of three months. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Japan Is the First to Be Affected 21

Silk Prices Plunge, US Dollar Exchange Temporarily Suspended

(Tokyo) The Japanese financial community is particularly concerned about the US financial panic. There are two opinions on its future prospects: one is that the United States will definitely ban gold exports, and the other is that it will continue to adopt a free policy. The reason for banning exports is to reduce the market price of gold and help the domestic economy boom, resisting imports. The observation of the free policy is that the United States has an overabundance of gold reserves, and even if it adopts a policy of devaluing currency, it will be difficult to create a boom. The Japanese financial community is particularly worried about the United States adopting a policy of banning gold exports, because doing so would eliminate Japan's foreign exchange boom and cause panic in Japanese rural areas. (United Press dispatch, 5th)

(Tokyo) The US financial panic has affected the entire country. 80 to 90% of Japanese raw silk is sold to the United States, so market prices have plummeted. If the exchange rate against the US dollar falls to 25 cents, the losses suffered by foreign export trade in the second half of the year will be enormous. Key figures from the Japanese Ministry of Finance and the financial community have convened emergency meetings to discuss countermeasures. Because the US countermeasures have not been determined, Japan has not decided on the final countermeasures. Banks will temporarily suspend foreign exchange with the US tomorrow, and the countermeasures after the 7th will be discussed again tomorrow. (United Press dispatch, 5th)

Gu Weijun Meets with Paul-Boncour 22

Inquires about France's Opinion on Sanctions and Arms Embargo

Says Will Maintain Same Stance as US and League of Nations

Havas Geneva Dispatch, 4th. French representative Paul-Boncour departs for home tonight. Prior to his departure, he discussed the work of the Disarmament Conference with Conference Chairman Henderson. He also met with Gu Weijun, the chief representative of China to the League of Nations, and Hu Shize, the Chinese envoy to Switzerland. The purpose of the Chinese representatives' visit to Paul-Boncour was to inquire about the French government's opinion on the situation in Rehe. At the last session of the League of Nations Assembly, Gu Weijun, based on the unanimous passage of the Nineteenth Committee report, requested the League of Nations to implement the various sanction provisions of Article 16 of the Covenant. It is believed that the purpose of the Chinese representatives' visit was to ascertain France's intentions regarding sanctions and the implementation of a ban on arms shipments to the Far East. According to Havas, Paul-Boncour only replied to the Chinese representatives that France would take the same stance as the member states of the League of Nations and the United States.

Japan Shows Goodwill to the Netherlands 24

Japanese Ambassador to the Netherlands Says:

No War between US and Japan, East Indies Can Be at Peace

Reuters The Hague Dispatch, 4th. The new Japanese ambassador to the Netherlands, Saito, told a Reuters reporter here that Matsuoka's visit to the Netherlands was of a private nature. He would only stay for a few days and then go to London. There was no question of negotiating a non-aggression pact between the two countries with the Dutch government. There was no reason for the Dutch East Indies to be apprehensive. The oil stations on Borneo were indeed important to the Japanese Navy, but it would only be a matter of life and death if there was a conflict between the United States and Japan in the Atlantic Ocean. He said that there would never be a war between the United States and Japan that would make it necessary for Japan to lack a way to ensure oil supply. Japan adopted a friendly policy towards the Dutch Indies.

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Drafts

Withdrawal from the League of Nations Notification 25

To Be Consulted by the Privy Council After Today's Cabinet Meeting

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs' proposal on withdrawing from the League of Nations has been finalized. A meeting of key officials will be held on the morning of the 6th to finalize it, and then a temporary cabinet meeting will decide it in the afternoon, after which the process of consulting the Privy Council will be adopted. According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' plan, the notification of withdrawal from the League of Nations and its reasons are not separated. Only in the notification of withdrawal to the Secretariat are the shortcomings of the League of Nations and the impropriety of handling the Sino-Japanese dispute pointed out, and the reasons for withdrawal are recorded. The notification is written in Japanese, simple and clear, with only 1,500 characters. When the notification is submitted, the government's statement on the withdrawal will not be issued, and the notification will be used instead. The notification will be submitted to the Secretariat at the same time as it is published by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The Privy Council must be consulted as soon as possible. If the consultation is completed within one week, the Emperor will be asked to approve it on the 15th or 16th, and the notification will be submitted to the Secretariat of the League of Nations. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

(Tokyo) It is said that when the Japanese government formally notifies the League of Nations of its withdrawal, it will attach a statement saying that although Japan has had to withdraw from the League of Nations because of differences of opinion with the League of Nations on how to maintain peace in the Far East, Japan is still willing to do its utmost to promote international cooperation in order to maintain world peace. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Our Country's Coastal

Deployment of Japanese Navy 26

38 Warships, 8,000 Personnel

Second Task Force Fully Stationed at Qinhuangdao

Third Task Force Stationed in the Yangtze River, Sending Ships to Guard Southern China

(Tokyo) Regarding the Chinese coast guard, the Ministry of the Navy released information at 4:00 AM this morning. (Ministry of the Navy Announcement) At the end of last year, the Outer Fleet, commanded by Rear Admiral Tsuji, which was responsible for guarding the coast of North China [Manchukuo], originally consisted of the warship Hirato and three destroyers of the Sixteenth Destroyer Squadron. After the Shanhaiguan Incident, the warship Tokiwa was added. At the time of the Japanese [Manchu] army's [invasion] of Rehe, fearing anti-Japanese behavior, the necessary deployment was made to protect Japanese residents. The special service ship Kamui departed Sasebo on January 28, the warship Tama departed Maizuru on February 28, and four destroyers of the Fifteenth Destroyer Squadron departed Kure, all joining the Second Outer Fleet. (1) Because the coast of Shanhaiguan, Qinhuangdao, and Dagu is frozen, it is very difficult for warships to move, but the maritime guard is still very complete. Currently, with the exception of the Tokiwa in Qingdao, the entire Second Outer Fleet is guarding Shanhaiguan and Bohai Island. The Third Fleet is guarding the Yangtze River basin, and the Magong Naval Base fleet is guarding the coast of southern China. The total naval force is 38 warships and more than 8,000 personnel. So far, there have been no accidents. (Dentsu dispatch, 5th)

A Certain Legal Expert Discusses the Question of Sino-Japanese Severance of Relations 29

(Nanjing) On the 5th, the reporter met with a certain legal expert and discussed international law, as well as the severance of Sino-Japanese relations. He said that before severing relations, we should consider the following questions: (1) Suppose we send the Japanese ambassador back to his country, and he relocates to the Shanghai Concession, what will we do?

(2) Can we recover the Japanese concessions in China, and can the unequal treaties be abolished? (3) How can we prevent Japanese warships from sailing and docking in our territorial waters and ports? (4) Can troops stationed in China be expelled? (5) If they use this as an excuse to launch a large-scale invasion, how will we resist? (6) If the League of Nations considers this an act of escalation, or even a step towards war, will our international status be affected? (7) Even if the incident escalates, will the League of Nations invoke Article 16 of the Covenant? The above are all matters that must be considered in advance. (Central News Agency dispatch, 5th)

Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday

Ministry of Military Affairs Sends Advisory to Provincial and Municipal Governments to Preserve City Walls and Moats 32

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Military Affairs, believing that city walls are related to national defense and should not be easily demolished, has consulted with the Ministry of the Interior and sent an advisory to provincial and municipal governments that, with the exception of city walls and moats that have already been demolished or filled in various places, all city walls, moats, and border fortresses in various places should be preserved. If the development of municipal administration or important construction is hindered and the city walls and moats have lost their effectiveness, the local city government must submit a request to the Executive Yuan, which will forward it to the military and internal affairs departments for review. Only after approval may a certain part of the city walls or moats be demolished or filled. If city walls are damaged in various places, the local government will be instructed to repair them at any time. The gun emplacements on the city walls must be gradually improved for practical use. (Special dispatch, 5th)

Su Ma's Troops Transported from Moscow to Xinjiang 35

Public Telegram 68

Hankou Telegram. Please forward to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government's various ministries and departments. Also, to the Shanghai Aviation Association, the provincial and municipal governments and party headquarters, various national aviation salvation groups, and various legal entities. The Battle of Rehe has entered a phase of close combat. The war reports of late show that our hundreds of thousands of patriotic soldiers are fighting fiercely on the frontiers. The enemy's strong armor and sharp weapons have become ineffective. If we can have 500 aircraft to fight a decisive battle with the Japanese invaders, it will not be difficult to recover Liaoning and Shenyang. The people of the country, alarmed by the tragic bombing of Shanghai by enemy planes last year on January 28th, have initiated a national aviation salvation movement. The news has spread, and the country is in shock. The people of Hubei, patriotic, dare not lag behind. Therefore, on February 25th, the Hubei Provincial National Air Force Founding Association was formally established in Hankou, and branches were established in various counties and cities, aiming to recruit 600,000 members and raise funds for 15 aircraft in the shortest possible time, following the example of other provinces. However, in recent years, national salvation movements often start strong but end weak, with poor planning leading to little success. We now present three matters for the government and various national aviation salvation groups to pay close attention to, so that funds are not wasted and things can be realized: (1) Please implement the resolutions of the Second and Third Plenary Sessions of this session and unify the administrative construction of aviation. The provinces are each establishing their own forces, each seeking development, with talent and machinery forming their own factions. The orders of the central government are not followed, and the tragedy of internal strife can be expected. Even if China has 3,000 aircraft, the result could still be national demise. (2) Please unify the aviation salvation organizations in various provinces and strive for overall development. We advocate long-term resistance against Japan and must first have the people voluntarily establish the air force. The initial total should be 500 aircraft, with large provinces raising funds for 50 aircraft and small provinces raising funds for 30 aircraft. Each province should have a general association, and each county and city should have a branch. All organizations and groups should be automatic members. The country should have 10 million members, each donating 5 yuan. In the future, the people can donate 500 aircraft to the government each year. (3) Please ensure that the funds raised by the provinces and counties are fully concentrated in the provincial capitals by August of the 22nd year, with people of the highest reputation publicly elected to be responsible for safekeeping. At the same time, please designate the highest fund-receiving agency of the government and periodically convene representatives from the provinces responsible for safekeeping donations to the capital, together with aviation authorities, to determine the procedures for establishing the air force, so that by the end of the 22nd year, we will have 500 aircraft defending our airspace, flying in the sky. Although the people of Hubei have suffered through military calamity, we are willing to work together with our compatriots throughout the country to achieve this. The Hubei Provincial National Air Force Founding Association respectfully petitions.

Russian Counter-Revolutionary Conspiracy Exposed 69

Attempting to Sabotage Agricultural Production and Create Famine

Hitler's Anti-Communist Rhetoric

Provokes Repercussions in Russian Newspapers

TASS, Moscow, 5th. According to an announcement by the State Political Department today, seventy people have been detained for engaging in counter-revolutionary activities. During interrogation, they confessed that they were plotting to sabotage agricultural production and create famine. Agencies of the State Political Department have recently uncovered many counter-revolutionary sabotage organizations. These organizations are mostly hidden within a portion of the agencies of the Agricultural Commission and the State Farm Commission, especially in Ukraine, the North Caucasus, and various agricultural regions of Russia. The majority of their members are employees of state-run agencies, all from landlord backgrounds. Most of those arrested confessed to engaging in counter-revolutionary activities, plotting to sabotage agriculture. Their methods include damaging motor vehicles and other agricultural machinery, accumulating weeds, engaging in slow-downs and arson in motor vehicle yards and flax mills to reduce production, robbing collective farm grains, disrupting planting and harvesting movements, and plotting to murder livestock, etc.

TASS, Moscow, 5th. German Chancellor Hitler's speech attacking the Soviet Union has provoked a strong reaction in the Soviet Union. The Soviet government's bulletin [Izvestia] today published a sharp editorial under the title [Clumsy Fool], saying, "Even with intimidation and provocation, the leaders of the National Socialist Party have clearly failed to fully control their chances of success in the election. Therefore, in addition to batons and machine guns, they are also trying to use their theoretical rhetoric on the eve of the election." On March 3rd, Mr. Hitler delivered a lengthy policy declaration. Everyone hoped that Mr. Hitler could state his plan to save Germany from its current dangerous situation, but the result was that he only used the Soviet Union as an example to prove the tragic results of communism. Although we do not want to respond to Mr. Hitler's [analysis] of the Soviet Union's situation, under these circumstances, even if German politicians do not want to save all their people, they at least want to save the German nation. Since Mr. Hitler has raised this [discussion], he should not blame us for being forced to respond. In recent years, the leading economists of the capitalist world have come to the Soviet Union to study its economic development. Even bourgeois scientists and politicians are discussing the possibility of implementing the Soviet Union's planned economic experiment in capitalist lands. This is not because of the collapse of the Soviet economy or the hardship of the Soviet people, but because of the development of the socialist economy, the elimination of unemployment, and the progress of Soviet culture. Mr. Hitler does not mention a word about the Soviet Union's collective agricultural construction, but wants to scare the Germans with stories about Soviet terror. The world's listeners will surely laugh at this. The National Socialist Party members call themselves German patriots and believe that they can better protect Germany's interests than others, but the policies they are pursuing are exactly the opposite, such as organizing civil war and launching indiscriminate attacks against the Soviet Union, the only country that does not harbor hostility towards Germany. They believe that this is a wise move, but we believe that with such National Socialist gentlemen at the helm, Germany's ship may not reach its destination." [Pravda] published an editorial titled [The Clown Takes the Stage], claiming that no one is unaware that the Reichstag fire was a provocative act by the National Socialists. All kinds of evidence prove that this is a re-enactment of the French Gogol affair. Hitler has only been in power for a month, but in this short period, the National Socialists have used every means to oppress German workers and peasants. In fact, the National Socialist forces' instigation of civil war will only increase Germany's internal strife, and the results of their foreign policy will be even more tragic. In just thirty days, those who call themselves [representatives of the nation] have clashed with the entire world. If they cannot carefully choose a different path, the newspaper concludes, "The party that bears the name [National] is isolating Germany and weakening its international position. Only such clownish policies can isolate Germany, but those who embrace such policies will probably not last long."

Turmoil in the Austrian Parliament 70

Government Party Disadvantaged in Vote on Motion

Speaker and Deputy Speaker of the House Resign

Havas, Vienna, 4th. The House of Representatives held an extraordinary meeting today. At the close of the meeting, the Speaker and Deputy Speaker resigned, much to the surprise of the general public. The Greater German Party introduced a motion demanding leniency towards striking workers. The House voted on the motion, passing it by a vote of 81 to 80. The Greater German Party, with the support of the Social Democratic Party, caused the government parties to become the minority. The Christian Social Party, which belongs to the government faction, was quite disadvantaged. At that time, the noise in the chamber became even louder, and the Speaker announced the adjournment of the meeting and withdrew to consult with the Deputy Speaker. When the meeting was reconvened, they both submitted their resignations.

The Secret of the Swallows' Nest 74

A Couch Full of Female Guests

Reuters, Belgrade Correspondence. The police here discovered an opium den outside the city of Belgrade. This matter was discovered by a female detective. She saw the wife enter a very luxurious and spacious villa. German General Election Held 75

Storm Troopers Armed Watch, Berlin Silent

Communists Concealed, But Secret Struggle Still Fierce

Germany's Future Fate Tied to This Result

Guomin, Berlin, 5th. Today is General Election Day. The morning passed quietly, indistinguishable from an ordinary Sunday, except that the election affairs, which are usually set up in front of public buildings, today have National Defense Party Storm Troopers and Steel Helmet members standing guard with their uniforms erect. Plainclothesmen also carried slogan boards of the Social Democratic Party and other parties, running around. In the last election, the Communist Party was the most powerful party. Today, even in the streets of the labor districts, they have disappeared. All the labor districts are unusually quiet, apparently due to special orders issued by the Communist Party leaders. But although the surface is quiet, the struggle is still going on. Judging from the current situation, the number of votes cast this time will certainly exceed the previous two elections. Havas, Warsaw, 5th. According to unconfirmed news from Berlin, the city of Berlin was extremely quiet this morning, with few pedestrians on the streets. However, most of the members of the National Socialist Storm Troopers were divided into several small groups, each group of about three or four people, as well as police and supplemental police, patrolling slowly on the main roads of the capital. At the street corners, police officers stood guard with Mauser rifles. At the entrance of the polling places, news vendors stood shoulder to shoulder with badges of various parties, without any discord, which shows that the situation is stable. President Hindenburg, accompanied by Secretary-General Meissner, went to a polling place nearby in the early morning to vote. When the President's ballot was dropped into the ballot box, some people cheered and welcomed him, as usual. Among them, some shouted [God bless you]. When the President slowly boarded the car and paid tribute to the crowd, photographers scrambled to take pictures. Vice-Chancellor Papen followed to the polling place shortly after. Foreign Minister Neurath also arrived soon after. The cabinet ministers Goring, Interior Minister Frick, and several other National Socialist cabinet members voted at another polling place.

Reuters, Berlin, 5th. The result of this election will determine the fate of Germany in the coming years, so everyone is extremely excited, especially in Berlin. The only question in the election district is the nation: Does it want Hitlerism? It is very difficult to predict the answer to this question. Hitler will certainly get the support of millions of people today, because only the National Socialist Party and its comrades were able to conduct organized propaganda. The Socialist Party and the Communist Party only relied on word of mouth. But Hitler may get an unexpected and unpleasant surprise. Now, looking at the labor districts of Berlin and other major cities, the workers are extremely jealous of Hitler, so they will never vote for Hitler. In past elections, many workers' homes flew red flags, but now they have disappeared, fearing insults from the National Socialist Storm Troopers. Many people expect that the Communist Party will not vote for its own party but will change to elect Socialist members, fearing that the votes cast by the Communist Party will be declared invalid. If so, the number of seats won by the Socialist Party will certainly increase. In addition, the number of seats won by the People's Party will also increase greatly, because former Chancellor Papen and Sellde are very popular among the middle class. As for the National Socialist Party, it may not be able to get 250 seats as in the election of July last year. According to this prediction, the right-wing parties combined may not be able to get the 51% of the total votes they hoped for. However, the abnormal situation and the [possible pressure] of the National Socialist brownshirts outside the polling places may greatly change this prediction. The police will serve the entire day to maintain order, and the brownshirts will help. The sale of alcohol is prohibited throughout the country today, as usual. The results of the election will not be known until late at night.

400 Communists Arrested Overnight Yesterday

Guomin, Berlin, 4th. The more liberal elements in the German government, seeing that the atmosphere in Europe cannot tolerate Chancellor Hitler's iron-fisted politics, are trying their best to stop Hitler and Goring from taking radical measures. But the Nazi Party's search and arrest of Communists has again created a new record in Prussia and throughout Germany today. Four hundred people were arrested in 24 hours. Since the Reichstag fire, no less than 4,000 people have been arrested. It is now rumored that Hitler intends to remain Chancellor regardless of the results of tomorrow's general election, and will begin a German rearmament plan, citing Geneva's failure to achieve military equality as a reason. France is said to be very alarmed by this, and most countries in Europe are also showing signs of shock and danger over Germany's recent developments.

Hitler's Last Campaign Speech

Guomin, Königsberg, 4th. German Chancellor Hitler gave a one-hour final election speech tonight, declaring, "We want to see the completion of national affairs in peace, but we are determined to protect the survival of the nation." At the same time, Hitler's brownshirts held lantern parades in more than a hundred cities and towns, and lit huge torches on the mountain peaks on the German border, indicating that the party leader was awakening national will.

The Mechanization of Soviet Agriculture (Part 2) 78

Soviet Correspondence (January 15th)

Extent of Agricultural Mechanization: The so-called agricultural mechanization is the application of machines to operate all agricultural production processes, such as plowing, sowing, harvesting, threshing, and fertilizing, and to exclude manual labor. This is also called agricultural industrialization.

Agricultural industrialization has not yet been achieved in backward countries, let alone advanced capitalist countries, because capitalists are unwilling to invest in agriculture due to natural conditions (climate) and social conditions (private land ownership, divided into small plots). On the farmers' side, most are small economies and unable to purchase machines. Therefore, under capitalism, a distinct difference has formed between advanced cities and backward rural areas.

Since the revolution, the Soviet Union has nationalized land. And since the implementation of the Five-Year Plan, most farmers have been collectivized, so the fields in the countryside have become vast and without small plots. In other words, the prerequisite conditions for agricultural mechanization have been met. Therefore, the current economic policy of the Soviet Union, in essence, is to vigorously eliminate this difference left over from the previous society and implement large-scale agricultural mechanization.

The main driving force of agricultural mechanization is tractors, which drive the above-mentioned various operating machines. Because the situation in the fields is different from that in factories, Lenin dreamed that there should be 100,000 tractors working in the Soviet countryside. But by the end of 1932, there were already 147,800 tractors working in Soviet agriculture (compared to only 26,700 in 1928), serving 6.82 million households, accounting for 24.9% of all farm households. These farm households have all joined collective farms. It goes without saying that state-owned farms, which play a significant role in Soviet agriculture, are fully mechanized.

In 1928, one-third of all farm households in the Soviet Union were still using wooden plows to cultivate the land, which had been passed down for thousands of years. But by 1932, this type of wooden plow had been abandoned in the Soviet countryside. 48% of the total sown area and 53% of the spring sown area were cultivated by tractor plows. In addition, the number of farm households using horse-drawn machinery was only 287,000 in 1928, accounting for 1.8% of all farm households. By 1932, it had increased to 7.5 million households, accounting for 30.5% of all farm households.

Also, in 1928, three-quarters of the spring sown area in the Soviet Union was sown by hand. By 1932, the main sowing tool had become a seed drill, accounting for about 40% of the spring sown area. In 1928, the area harvested with old-fashioned sickles reached 44 million hectares. In 1932, the main harvesting equipment for grains had become tractor-drawn harvesters and new-style combine harvesters. Similarly, in 1928, 40 million meters of harvest were threshed using flails and other manual threshing methods. By 1932, the main equipment had become tractor-drawn threshers and combine harvesters.

In short, half of the current agricultural production process in the Soviet Union has been mechanized. Especially in terms of quality, it is noted that the mechanization is not of individual farmers, but of collective farms and state-owned farms. This means that the higher the degree of collectivization of farmers, the greater the degree of mechanization.

In terms of region, the agricultural areas such as Ukraine and the North Caucasus have the highest degree of mechanization. For example, in terms of the number of tractors in each region, Ukraine has 18.3% of all tractors in the Soviet Union, the North Caucasus has 12.2%, the Central Volga has 9%, the Lower Volga has 7.5%, Western Siberia has 8.5%, Central Asia has 7.5%, and Kazakhstan has 5.1%. Furthermore, in terms of the value of all agricultural machinery in the Soviet Union, it totaled 1.449 billion rubles in 1928 (calculated at 1926-27 prices) and had increased to 2.3 billion rubles by 1932. During the first Five-Year Plan, machinery applied to agriculture totaled 1.6 billion rubles. In 1928, all machinery in agriculture was worth only 1.149 billion rubles. From this, one can imagine the rapid advancement of agricultural mechanization.

The Lever of Agricultural Mechanization: Machine and Tractor Stations. The lever for implementing agricultural mechanization in the Soviet Union is the Machine and Tractor Station. It is run by the government in suitable locations selected in agricultural areas, and its role is extremely significant. The most important aspects are described below.

(1) It can promote the collective farm movement. Soviet publications claim that "Machine and Tractor Stations are the true organizers of collectivization." This is because when farmers in a village have just established a collective farm, they may not be able to afford to purchase machines. They can rent them from the Machine and Tractor Station, and the rent is paid after the harvest. At this time, poor and middle peasants who have not yet joined the collective farm see the benefits of using machines for cultivation and are willing to join. (2) Machines are concentrated together, and their efficiency is greatly increased. For example, in 1928, collective farms owned a total of 20,000 tractors, which served only 45,000 farm households. In 1932, collective farms and Machine and Tractor Stations owned 85,000 tractors. Due to the establishment of Machine and Tractor Stations, the number of farm households served (all of whom had joined collective farms) reached 6.82 million. Moreover, the 6.8 million collective farm peasants served by Machine and Tractor Stations had a sown area of 35.3 million hectares, which is an average of 5.18 hectares per household. The 8.1 million collective farm peasants not served by Machine and Tractor Stations had a sown area of 31.4 million hectares, which is an average of 3.9 hectares per household. The 10 million individual farmers had a sown area of 19.8 million hectares, which is an average of only 1.98 hectares per household. From this, it can be seen that the labor productivity of collective farm households served by Machine and Tractor Stations is two and a half times higher than that of individual farmers and 37% higher than that of collective farm households not served by Machine and Tractor Stations. The effectiveness of Machine and Tractor Stations can be imagined.

It can implement state leadership over collective farms. Therefore, the so-called implementation of agricultural mechanization in the Soviet Union is mainly to develop this network of Machine and Tractor Stations. In 1928, there was only one such Machine and Tractor Station. In 1930, there were 158. In 1932, there were 2,498, with a total horsepower of 938,000, serving 40% of collective farms.

At the same time, Machine and Tractor Stations have become the political and cultural center of the Soviet countryside. Each station is equipped with hospitals, schools, cinemas, clubs, libraries, etc. In addition, the offices of party and government agencies are also located here. This plays a significant role in eliminating the differences between cities and rural areas.

Tractor drivers and other various machine operators are all trained by Machine and Tractor Stations. In 1931, the number of people entering training classes for tractor, combine harvester, and automobile drivers reached more than one million. In 1932, it had increased to more than 2.5 million.

The Outline of Agricultural Mechanization in the Second Five-Year Plan. The Second Five-Year Plan decided that by 1937, all farmers must be collectivized and agricultural production must be fully mechanized. The lever of mechanization | Machine and Tractor Stations will be increased to 5,500 to 6,000 by the end of the Second Five-Year Plan. It is planned that by the spring of 1934, all collective farms will be covered by the network of Machine and Tractor Stations.

During the Second Five-Year Plan, the Soviet Union can manufacture more than 170,000 tractors each year. Full agricultural mechanization is expected to require 15 million horsepower. The required tractors can be fully supplied by domestic manufacturers. Other auxiliary equipment is expected to cost 9 billion to 10 billion rubles, which is ten to eleven times more than the output in 1932.

Related to agricultural mechanization is the fuel problem. The only fuel currently used by tractors is petroleum. By the end of the Second Five-Year Plan, the 15 million horsepower required for agricultural mechanization will require 15 million tons of gasoline. To refine such a huge amount of gasoline, 45 million tons of crude oil are required. This will account for half of the planned oil production in 1937.

In addition, during the Second Five-Year Plan, it is stipulated that a portion of agricultural production must be electrified. By 1937, at least 9 billion to 10 billion kilowatt-hours of electricity must be applied to agriculture. It is planned to first electrify dairy products, state-owned and group beekeeping farms, followed by industrial crops such as cotton, hemp, sugar, and turnips. At most, 3 to 4 million hectares of field operations will be electrified.

Li Lieh-chun's Proposal 79

| Matters related to military secrets will not be published |

Central Committee member Li Lieh-chun was summoned to Beijing. It is said that he has an important proposal. Various newspapers have briefly reported on it, but the details are unknown. The results of the central government's discussion are also unknown. Now, with Li's consent, the reporter publishes a part of it, which is recorded as follows: [In the history of various countries in the world, the ages are different, and the positions of prosperity are also different. Internal worries and external troubles are almost universal to all countries. Those who do not handle them well will perish, and those who handle them well will turn misfortune into good fortune. Historical traces are numerous and cannot be listed exhaustively. However, when a country is in danger, the reason why it can turn danger into safety and chaos into order is that there is a kind of national spirit that runs through it. Internally, it can make great reforms, and externally, it can make great struggles. The situation in which our country finds itself today cannot be said to be not serious. If we want to break through this difficult situation and cross to the other shore, then we can only make great reforms in internal affairs and great struggles against foreign aggression, and only by consistently implementing this spirit can we succeed. I, Lieh-chun, went to Beijing to participate in the final discussion. I was ordered to accept the teachings, which is what I wanted. However, I cannot remain silent about my foolish thoughts. The proposals are as follows:

A. Regarding the minimum preparations for resisting foreign aggression, military affairs, finance, and diplomacy (there are eight items in total, which are omitted due to confidentiality). As for the military aspects of the national defense plan, the matter is very complicated. I heard that the competent authorities already have a considerable plan, but giving it practical implementation will surely benefit the actual situation. I will only choose a few matters to speak about. No matter what the plan is, there must be a superior military force and talent, weapons and materials, and huge economic resources and necessary military expenses must be fully prepared. And there must be a considerable amount of time before it can be successful. Of the matters described above, the economy is the most difficult. Although, even a small country like Japan can bear a national debt of more than 70 billion yuan. The domestic public debt, even this time of issuance, is quite large for the enemy. How can it be said that China, with its vastness and the patriotism of its people, is not as good as Japan? Even with frequent disasters, it should be able to raise huge national defense public bonds to relieve the national crisis and resist the violent Japan. The obligation and the right go hand in hand. If only the obligation is fulfilled and the right is not enjoyed, and even all facilities are contrary to the spirit of the Republic, then the people are treated as slaves. How can this succeed? If we can reverse this and make the people directly and indirectly work hard for national affairs, and the government and the people all follow the correct path of the Republic, then the intelligence of the people of the whole country will surely be gathered, and it will not be difficult to save the country and revitalize it. However, during this period, the minimum limit must be able to implement the following matters:

B. Regarding the minimum facilities for reforming internal affairs (1) Enforce the complete freedom of the people to assemble, associate, speak, publish, reside, and believe, and cancel the laws that hinder the aforementioned items. Officials and party departments in various places who have hindered the aforementioned actions shall be prohibited and severely punished separately. Clearly permit the people to freely organize political parties, but during the period of political tutelage, it must be within the scope of being able to abide by the Three Principles of the People. (2) The National Political Consultative Conference should be entirely elected by the people, and its rights should be like those of the lower house of various countries, resolving national affairs. (3) Expand the power of local autonomy. The people of each county shall elect county officials to carry out the political affairs of a county, and elect councilors to discuss and establish the laws of a county. Provincial governors of all provinces shall simultaneously implement popular elections. The aforementioned (A) items are necessary for resisting Japan. However, if (B) items are not resolutely implemented, then (A) items will be difficult to fully realize. And the things stated in (B) are already within the scope of this party, and are old tunes repeated, and are the most ordinary things. It is a matter of being able to implement them. When the national crisis has reached this point, I know that this party will definitely be able to use them. If it can be like this, then the people's attitude towards national affairs will surely change from pessimism to optimism, from passivity to activism. When factionalism is eliminated, the talents of the whole country will naturally gather. How can there be a situation where foreign troubles are not eliminated, the foundation of the country is not consolidated, and things are not improving day by day? It is a matter of sincerely planning for it. Therefore, I have prepared a brief statement and respectfully present it for public inspection and decide to implement it.

Fundraising Methods Have Been Decided

Jinan Correspondence: The Airplane Donation Committee organized by various party, military, and political circles in this city, after appointing Han Fu-chu, Zhang Wei-cun, Li Tian-ni, and others as 21 standing committee members, held its first standing committee meeting yesterday (the 3rd) at 2:00 PM at the provincial party headquarters. (2) The fundraising methods have been drafted by the fundraising team. The discussion items: (1) Is the fundraising method drafted by the fundraising team appropriate? Please make a public decision. The case was discussed, amended, and passed. The fundraising methods are as follows: (1) Methods for donations from civil servants (party, government, military, and police) (limited to three months): 1. Those with monthly salaries of 50 yuan or more to 100 yuan, donate 2% per month. 2. Those with monthly salaries of 101 yuan to 200 yuan, donate 6% per month. 3. Those with monthly salaries of 201 yuan to 300 yuan, donate 8% per month. 4. Those with monthly salaries of 301 yuan or more, donate 10% per month. (2) Business community: 1. Donate one month's worth of business tax, collected separately by the chairmen of each industry association. 2. Special fundraising from wealthy households. 3. Special fundraising from banks, factories, and guild halls. (3) Academic community: 1. Teachers and staff of all levels of schools should follow the donation methods for civil servants. 2. Students of all levels of schools will be encouraged to donate by the county party headquarters in conjunction with the principals of all levels of schools. (4) Workers: The county party headquarters will cooperate with the responsible persons of various labor unions or factory managers to encourage donations. (5) Citizens: 1. The municipal government will levy an additional month's worth of house tax. 2. The municipal government will instruct the Public Security Bureau to cooperate with the chiefs of each district and neighborhood to encourage donations from door to door. 3. Special fundraising from wealthy and reputable households in the city. (6) An additional 10% of entertainment tax will be levied on all entertainment venues for a period of three months. (7) Voluntary donations: Entrust various newspapers in the city to encourage donations and collect funds on behalf of the committee. (8) These methods will be implemented starting in March.

Activities of Japanese Warships Stationed in Wuhu 82

Fushimi and Toba Come and Go

Japanese Consul in Wuhu Suddenly Requests Protection of Overseas Chinese

Wuhu correspondence: Recently, Japanese naval officers and soldiers stationed in Wuhu, as well as Japanese people residing in Wuhu, have been very active. They have been going ashore for sightseeing, secretly surveying the terrain, and holding overseas Chinese conferences, as if preparing for an emergency. Unexpectedly, the Japanese warship Fushimi suddenly sailed downstream at 7:00 this morning, while the former Feiying warship stationed at Jiangguanmenzhou in Wuhu moved to the inside of the Osaka lighter ship. At 4:00 in the afternoon, the gunboat Toba arrived in Wuhu from downstream. According to Japanese officers on the ship, the two destroyers Momoyuki will come to Wuhu tomorrow. Two officers of the Toba warship went ashore to meet with Japanese Consul Shibazaki and Shirao at the Japanese Consulate. The Japanese consul then drove to the Second District Administrative Commissioner's Office to meet with Commissioner Gao Tie-jun to request protection of the lives and property of Japanese residents. Mr. Gao also asked them to restrain Japanese soldiers and residents and abide by order. After about half an hour of discussion, the Japanese consul left and inspected Zhongshan Road and Beiping Road. However, the public is very strange about the various actions of the Japanese soldiers and civilians and the sudden request of the Japanese consul for the protection of overseas Chinese. (4th)

Songjiang 83

The First District Vigorously Implements Universal Training

This county was ordered to organize a defense regiment. Universal training was implemented in early last month. The regimental soldiers who should be trained in various townships and towns in the first district were divided into four groups. They gathered for exercises at 7:00 every morning. Many people were able to report on time, but there were also quite a few who stopped halfway or made excuses to shirk their responsibilities. Tai Shi, the head of the first district, and Gu Yangtian, the head of the district regiment, specially convened a meeting of township and town leaders and Jia chiefs yesterday to explain the reasons for the establishment of the defense regiment and its relationship with local autonomy. As a result of the discussion, the regimental soldiers in each township and town who dropped out or shirked their responsibilities must be notified by the township and town chiefs and Jia chiefs together with the township and town police, and the reward and punishment measures of the defense regiment must be printed and actively publicized so that the regimental soldiers know what to be vigilant about. With this supervision, the universal training in the first district should be effective.

Taicang 84

Drugs

The Investigation Office Begins Operations

The Fifth Branch of the Jiangsu Provincial Drug Investigation Office has been established, using No. 101, Sixth Street, Dongmen Avenue as its office. Director Li Huchen has begun operations.

Two Burglaries in One Night 85

In the middle of the night on the 2nd of this month, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came to the home of Zhang Shaoqing, a farmer in Jiuliqiao, broke into the house, and searched and robbed at will, losing about 500 yuan worth of clothing and foreign goods. That night, the home of surgeon Zheng Yehan in Gutang outside the West Gate was also visited by more than 20 bandits, six or seven of whom were armed with pistols. Fortunately, the family discovered it early and rang the gong for help. Zheng Yehan held a self-defense gun and opened fire on the bandits. Seeing that their efforts were not working well, the bandits took advantage of the pre-arranged boats and fled west.

Wuxi 86

Designated Sales Area for Refined Salt

The Ministry of Finance, in view of the dispute between Changzhou Jing Shang and Jiuda Company over the sale of refined salt in Wuxi, previously presented an order from the Executive Yuan, stipulating that the prosperous roads in the Muyi, Yingyun, Kaiyuan, and Liangxiang areas should be the scope of Wuxi's refined salt sales. It was instructed to comply with the record. Later, Changzhou Jing Shang and the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce and others appealed that they could not accurately prove the boundaries of the original commercial port. They should submit another request to the Executive Yuan for approval. The Executive Yuan then instructed, "After investigation by the ministry, and according to the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce and Yang Shou-nan, the boundaries of the original commercial port could not be accurately proven, and the market conditions have changed greatly after many years. The area previously designated by the Executive Yuan should still be the scope of the refined salt sales area." Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Envoy's Office to forward a letter to the local county government for information, and requested assistance in delineating the boundaries of the Wuxi commercial port area.

Changzhou 87

Construction of Yong'an River Begins

The Yong'an River in the 19th District of Wu County connects Shao Yao Port in the south and Lao Du Port in the north, running more than 30 miles across. The river has been silted up since it was dredged in the early years of the Republic of China. The district head Zhu Ying and others specially initiated a dredging project by referring to the previous practice of collecting labor. The officials were designated to start the damming and construction yesterday (the 5th), and they reported to the county in advance for record and gave a notice.

The Department Orders the Construction of the Wuyi and Xiyi Roads

The Wu County Construction Bureau is preparing to carry out the Wuyi and Xiyi road projects. Recently, the bureau was ordered to be abolished, and the Construction Department specially ordered County Magistrate Zhang to continue to rush the construction of the earthwork of the two roads under the supervision of Director Zhi Wei, and to report the progress of the project in detail immediately.

Zhenjiang 88

Zhen Dan Jin

Regular Bus Service Scheduled

The Zhen Dan Jin Weituo Bus Company was established by gentry and businessmen from Danyang and Jintan counties. It has collected 50,000 yuan in capital and established a board of directors. On the 1st of this month, it signed an exclusive contract with the Construction Department. Recently, it has consulted with Zhenjiang gentry and businessmen to join the share capital and purchased six large and small buses. It is scheduled to officially start the service on March 15, first opening the Danyang to Jintan section, which is 50 miles long. The test runs have been very successful in recent days. The roads along the way are all paved with gravel and are well-maintained. It takes about 45 minutes to reach the destination, and the ticket price is only one yuan. In the future, when the route is extended to Liyang, it can be connected to the Beijing-Hangzhou Highway.

Verdict on Arson Case of Oil Tanker 89

Zhang Xiatang, the owner of the oil tanker of the Asia Petroleum Company, transported 3,000 boxes of kerosene in October last year and planned to deliver them to Suqian. In advance, he was instructed by an employee of the company to sell all the oil gradually after arriving in Gua and Yang. He put the ship into Shaobo Lake and set it on fire to try to destroy the evidence. Another owner, Chen Laoqi, received a reward of 2,000 yuan and fled. Zhang then reported to the police station. The police station detained Zhang Xiatang because the incident was bizarre and the circumstances did not match. While the investigation was underway, the company had received a secret report, found evidence, and detained Zhang and Zhou, the manager of Yangzhou, at the Public Security Bureau, and then transferred them to Zhenjiang. After being interrogated by the Security Department, they were transferred to the court for investigation. The case was recently concluded. Yesterday, Zhang was taken to the criminal court for interrogation. Judge Shen presided over the court and brought Zhang to the case. After questioning, he was sentenced to one year in prison. Zhang declared in court that he was not satisfied and prepared to appeal.

Huzhou 90

Detective Team Solves Two Theft Cases

Wu Xing County Public Security Bureau Detective Team Detective Chen You-ting led a number of detectives yesterday and arrested two major thieves, Gong Amao and Wang Bao-dai, at the home of a certain surname behind the guild hall outside the West Gate, along with more than 40 pieces of stolen goods and a pipe for smoking opium. They were all taken to the team for interrogation.

Ningbo 91

The 21st Division's Logistics Transports to Jiangxi

Liu Zhennian's troops of the 21st Division stationed in various parts of Wen Prefecture were ordered to open up bandits in eastern Jiangxi. Zhang Yulin and Kai Guang, the staff officers of the division headquarters, came to Yong from Wen yesterday. The Yong station prepared more than 60 vehicles to transport logistics and a large number of military vehicles. The logistics and other items were loaded onto the Songpu ship of the Sanbei Company this afternoon and transferred to the train, and then entered Jiangxi via the Hangjiang Road for bandit suppression. The various units of the division departed from their original defense areas in Wen Prefecture and entered Jiangxi via Longquan via land.
