Local News

Sun Ke Advocates That Zhang Xueliang Resign Quickly to Apologize to the People 92

Urges Chiang to Go North to Preside Over Military Affairs in North China

To Undertake Bandit Suppression Work in the Southwestern Provinces

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, met with reporters from various newspapers at his private residence on Columbia Road at 3:00 p.m. yesterday. He expressed extreme indignation over the entire fall of Rehe in less than ten days, saying that not only the military commanders such as Tang Yulin, who were in command at the front line, should be severely punished, but also Zhang Xueliang, who was most responsible, should immediately resign to apologize to the people. Otherwise, in order to maintain its prestige and discipline, the central government should make a determination and order Zhang to be removed from all his positions. At the same time, we should unanimously urge Commander Chiang to go north as soon as possible to preside over the reorganization and save the crisis, and said that he had telegraphed Chiang yesterday afternoon, urging him to return to Beijing immediately. The following is a record of Sun's remarks.

The War Lasted Less Than Ten Days 93

Sun said first that Rehe was a natural barrier, and the defending army numbered more than 100,000. Although the central government knew that the result would be defeat, it thought that it could at least last for two or three months. Zhang Hanqing also said to others that it would last for two months. During this period, it was enough to give our country's representative in Geneva an opportunity to work hard, so that the international community could develop more powerfully in sanctioning Japan. Unexpectedly, the war lasted less than ten days, and the entire front collapsed, and Chengde fell. It was really unexpected. Calculating that the Japanese army advanced 50 miles a day, as if entering an unmanned area, who can believe that it was resistance and that there was a fierce war? No wonder our overseas representatives repeatedly heard of the loss of important passes and believed that the generals defending the land were implementing the non-resistance policy, so they resigned in anger.

Zhang Should Resign Quickly 94

Victory or defeat in war is common for military strategists, but retreating without fighting is a great shame. As for the issue of responsibility for this war, the military commanders such as Tang Yulin, who were in command at the front line, should be directly responsible and should be severely punished. Zhang Xueliang, as the highest military commander in North China, should of course bear the greatest responsibility. He had already lost three provinces in one day and handed over Jinzhou. Recently, he lost Yuguan again. At that time, the people of the country still hoped that Zhang would atone for his crimes and be determined to defend Rehe and fight the enemy. As a result, the four northeastern provinces were lost and the troops under his command collapsed without fighting. He shirked his responsibility and was spurned by the whole country. For Zhang's sake, he can only resign quickly to apologize to the people, give way to the virtuous and able, and support the crisis in North China. If he continues to linger in his position, I personally advocate that the central government should make a determination and order his removal.

Telegram to Urge Chiang to Return to Beijing 95

In terms of the central government, the Rehe war was originally expected to last for two or three months, so Military Commander Chiang was stationed in Jiangxi to supervise the suppression of bandits because the bandits in Jiangxi were rampant. Now that Rehe has fallen and Pingjin is in critical condition, the situation in Chahar and Suiyuan is also in danger. Therefore, in terms of the situation, North China is more important and the Red bandits are less important. Therefore, we advocate that Chiang be invited to go north as soon as possible, and that troops be transferred from the southwestern provinces of Fujian and Hunan to be responsible for the work of suppressing bandits. Chiang is the highest military commander in the country, so the defense of North China can only be solved by Chiang's going north. I telegraphed Chiang this afternoon (that is, yesterday afternoon) to urge him to return to Beijing as soon as possible to work together to remedy the situation. I will also return to Beijing in the next few days.

Compromise Is Nonsense 96

When reporters asked about the issue of breaking off diplomatic relations with Japan, Sun said that our country's military is so uncompetitive, and even if breaking off diplomatic relations is realized, it will not help. When asked about the rumors that the central government and Japan are compromising, Sun firmly denied it, saying that at this time, unless one is insane, where would there be compromise? Sun finally said that all sectors are enthusiastic about saving the country and actively contributing, and he hopes that they will not be discouraged by the loss of Rehe. The central government has the determination to work together from top to bottom to deal with this unprecedented crisis.

Liu Chongjie's Heartbreaking Words 97

The Soldiers on the Front Line Are Not Competitive

What Diplomacy Can Be Talked About?

Yesterday morning, reporters met with Vice Foreign Minister Liu Chongjie. Liu expressed his sadness and indignation, saying that in today's situation, the soldiers on the front line are not competitive, so what is there to talk about? And the diplomatic backing is non-existent, so what diplomacy can be talked about? No wonder the three representatives of the League of Nations have expressed their indignation and resigned. Today's (that is, yesterday's) newspaper reported that Minister Luo resigned in anger due to the loss of Chengde. I have not received a confirmed report on this, so I will return to Beijing this afternoon (that is, yesterday). If Minister Luo really resigns, I will definitely not linger in my position. Liu also said that although the Japanese army's invasion of Rehe is determined to win, we should resolutely resist it no matter what. Now, they have left without fighting. This responsibility should not only be borne by Tang Yulin, but also by the military commanders in the front. Now that Rehe has been lost, the security of Pingjin is completely gone. Although the Japanese side has repeatedly stated that it will never invade Guannei, no one can guarantee the actions of the Japanese, and how can we predict that they will not have other plans in the Pingjin area?

Song Ziwen's Speech 98

Victory Comes from Failure

Deeply Hope That the People and Soldiers Will Be Awakened

Regarding the loss of Rehe, Dean Song published a speech as follows: After I returned from Rehe, the military commanders asked me for my personal observations on how long Rehe could be defended. I replied that it would be one week to ten days. At that time, those who heard my words laughed and said that even if the Japanese army drove straight in without any resistance, it would take several weeks to walk from the border of Rehe to Chengde. The ten-day period is ridiculous. I replied that the Japanese army's march cannot be calculated on foot. Tens of thousands or hundreds of thousands of troops are scattered. They travel dozens of miles a day. They use written and oral reports as official announcements of victory. There is very little real support. This is the concept of the old-fashioned tactics that our country's military personnel have always been full of. They have not deeply understood the new tactics of modern warfare, which require months of continuous rear preparation for the final battle of a few days. It is said that raising soldiers for a thousand days is for a day's use. This is an ancient principle that has been overturned in modern warfare. Unfortunately, our country's military has not paid attention to it. In the recent changes in Rehe, the Japanese army has railways for transportation in the rear and a strict logistics system, plus the active preparation of numbers, to make the final blow. Airplanes, tanks, armored vehicles, over-mountain guns, and cavalry come at the same time like a storm. Looking back at the army defending Rehe in our country, there is absolutely no so-called staff work. The military commanders are leisurely and slow to act. Ancient-style vehicles are used for transportation. It takes several weeks for camels and mules to transport from Beiping to the front line to reach the front line. There is no contact between the various troops, and there is no preparation for anti-aircraft guns and trenching tools. The soldiers have only received training in the drill field. Rehe is a natural barrier. If scientific tactics are used to defend it with danger, it is really a situation where one man can guard the pass. If it is still in the old style, it will become a dead end. For example, a narrow valley is the best target for airplanes and artillery. In addition, the command cannot be unified, and once it is defeated in a dangerous place, it will collapse and cannot be recovered. Rehe is the land of our Republic of China. How can it be handed over to others? The enemy is indeed stronger than us, but our soldiers defending the land are ordered by the government to resist and fight to the death with airplanes, tanks, and artillery for more than ten days with their flesh and blood. The brave and fearless spirit of our soldiers is far superior to that of the enemy, but what is lacking is tactics and equipment. As a result, Chengde was lost. After this bloody battle of more than ten days, it is enough to prove that the rumors that the generals of Rehe were colluding with the enemy are nonsense, and it is enough to prove that Rehe was not lost without fighting. The government ordered the army to resist, and no matter how much the army can defend, the government's policy cannot be criticized. There is a saying in Western languages: We do not necessarily fight to win, and even if we fight and lose, we can find a bright path in defeat. Now the army defending Rehe has been defeated, and everyone is pointing fingers at it. But when we ask ourselves, instead of blaming others, why not be self-aware? The Rehe war has given us a major lesson and a major awakening. The blame for the defeat is not on one person or a few people, but on the military system of our country. We raise soldiers for days and millions, but the equipment is inferior, the food and clothing are insufficient, and they are like a rabble. Even if the soldiers can risk their lives in danger, they are simply driving the people of the city to fight. The blame should be attributed to the poor military system. In European and American countries, those who join the army are excellent people, but in our country, it is not the case. Education is far behind others, and the youth are not trained, and there are very few excellent people who join the army. I dare to say that if our country's military does not quickly awaken, abandon the tactics of the 18th and 19th centuries, and strive for the training of modern troops, then national defense will ultimately be empty talk. But we must not be discouraged by this. Victory comes from failure. If the whole country is united and fights, the iron hooves of the invaders will surely produce a pure and bright national concept in us. The rise of the nation comes from blood and tears. Last year at this time, our army fought bravely against the invading Japanese army in Shanghai for more than 30 days. The world praised it and regarded it as a national hero. But a year later, tens of thousands of troops in Rehe collapsed in ten days, and the world's eyes have changed again. In fact, the army that resisted Japan in Shanghai last year and the army that is now defending the land in Rehe have the same origin. Why is there such a huge difference in strength and weakness? One is inspired by the national spirit, and the other is bound by primitive tactics and cannot save themselves. I deeply hope that the people and soldiers will gain a thorough awakening from the tragic lesson and seek a bright path for our nation.

The People of Shanghai Express Their Indignation at the Blame on the Volunteer Army for the Loss of Rehe 99

He Yinqiao and Others Send a Telegram

Call on Fellow Compatriots to Pay Attention

He Yinqiao and others sent a telegram, "To the Public Inspection of Various Newspapers: Recently, I read in today's newspapers that Chengde has been lost, and there are even telegrams claiming that, according to a spokesman for the Chinese authorities, the volunteer army refused to fight, etc. What the content is, those who care about the national crisis, based only on the reports in the newspapers, it is difficult to determine its authenticity. However, we calmly review the facts that have occurred since the September 18th Incident, weigh the situation and reason, and dare not believe this rumor. May I ask who has been persevering in resisting the enemy and fighting against Japan for the past year? Those who have been called to flow through the remote fortresses, unyielding and unyielding, to win back the personality of the nation and to awaken the loyal souls of the Chinese people, which one is not our iron-blooded man, the patriotic compatriots? As for losing three provinces without fighting in less than a day, giving up Jin and Yu without resistance, singing and dancing, and enjoying the sights and sounds, and recently issuing a telegram stating that they will mobilize, the whole country has not blamed them for their past mistakes, and has praised them as being generous. Who would have expected that they would hold their troops and not attack, with hundreds of thousands of troops under their command, and bear the full responsibility of defending the land, but would allow 120 Japanese soldiers to drive straight into the natural barrier of Rehe, blaming the volunteer army, and even saying that they did not fire a single shot. If they want the whole country to shift the blame in this way, Heaven, oh Heaven, is there such a reason? If we allow right and wrong to be unclear, then in the future, enthusiastic people will surely be heartbroken and disgusted by the name of the volunteer army, and will abandon it completely. It will destroy the enthusiasm for relieving the crisis and saving together, and cut off the source of funds and supplies, causing the heroic soldiers of Xue Dou to be shot and killed, and die tragically under the iron hooves of the enemy, causing the future of the nation to be irrevocably lost. The matter is so tragic that nothing can be worse than this. After investigating the Northeast Volunteer Army, who have risked their lives, they have been relying on the support of various circles at home and abroad to continue their struggle. The international community has paid attention to them, and the enemy has not dared to relax. Previously, I read the telegram news published in the Tianjin Dagong Daily and learned that the entire Rehe army was unified under the unified command of the Beiping Military Branch in the previous month. In the time when the government and the people are helping each other, these volunteer armies, who had previously defied all dangers, are now receiving the treatment of the national army, and the support seems to be worry-free. But now, when the strong enemy is in front of them, they do not fire a shot. Is there such a reason? The complexity of the matter cannot be explained in detail. I hope that the people of the country will explore quietly when reading the newspaper, and not rely on hearsay, so as not to be pained by those who are close to them and pleased by the enemies. The hearts of the people are said to be in danger, and we have to shout loudly and ask all compatriots to pay special attention. He Yinqiao, Wang Hegao, Chen Yian, and other 124 people kowtow together. "

Shanghai General Labor Union: In order to raise funds for the "Shanghai Workers' Plane," a discussion meeting was held at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, bringing together representatives from all sectors of the city's labor community to discuss practical implementation methods. There were more than 200 representatives from various labor unions. The details are recorded as follows:

Meeting Situation: After the meeting was announced, Zhu Xuefan was publicly elected as chairman, and Ye Gonglun as recorder. First, the chairman reported, saying roughly that the violent Japanese are invading the Northeast and are wreaking havoc with airplanes. Because our country lacks aviation weapons, although we have risen up to resist, we have ultimately failed to achieve victory in the war. The entire Shanghai labor community knows the importance of aviation to save the country, and the donation of airplanes cannot be delayed. Therefore, we plan to raise 100,000 yuan to raise a "Shanghai Workers' Plane" so that we can fulfill the duties of the city's labor community and complete the work of saving the country through aviation. All workers should rise up bravely. How to proceed to achieve success? We should ask the representatives to express their opinions and discuss them in detail, and so on. Then, Committee Member Li Yongxiang reported on the progress of raising funds for the "Shanghai Workers' Plane," and Zhu Xuefan reported on the enthusiastic support of the various labor unions. Then, representatives Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xianggao, Lu Muqin, Zhao Zhenhui, Li Mengnan, and others successively stood up to express their opinions and contribute various implementation plans to each other.

Resolutions: After the representatives expressed their opinions, the following resolutions were passed: (1) All labor unions must confirm their donations before the deadline and report to the meeting. (2) The deadline for payment of donations is one month, which may be extended if necessary. (3) Incentive measures will be formulated by the Fundraising Committee. (4) Donation items will be published in the newspaper daily to show good faith. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Grain, Flour and Oil Cake Trade Association: The Executive Committee held its 6th meeting of the second session yesterday afternoon. Wu Jingxiong Discusses Constitution Drafting 101

Preliminary Work to Be Completed Before the Sixth

Consideration Will Be Given to Opinions from All Parties

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency called on Mr. Wu Jingxiong, Vice Chairman of the Constitution Drafting Committee, at his private residence this morning to discuss the constitution drafting work. The details are recorded below:

Decided Sections: Mr. Wu said that the assumed sections are the territory, form of government, sovereignty, and flag colors discussed by the first group of the Constitution Drafting Committee. The territory is listed in the constitution, the form of government is the Republic of the Three Principles of the People, sovereignty belongs to the people, and the flag colors are Blue Sky, White Sun.

Under Discussion: Currently under discussion is the second group's rights of the people, obligations of the people, and people's livelihood. A meeting was held last Tuesday. There are many types of people's rights, and it was impossible to list them all at once. The ones that have been listed number as many as 18, which are similar to the 23 articles of Article 6 of the Provisional Constitution. The biggest difference is that Article 19 of the current Provisional Constitution stipulates that the people shall enjoy the right to inherit property in accordance with the law. The assumption of the subcommittee is to modify it to the people enjoy the right to inherit property, but the law may restrict it. In addition, Article 21 of the Provisional Constitution stipulates that the people have the right to sue in law in accordance with the law. The three words "in accordance with the law" are redundant. This law is the so-called constitution. The subcommittee assumes to modify it to the people have the right to sue in court in accordance with the law. The two words "in accordance with the law" refer to the law of procedure. The group is scheduled to continue the discussion on the 8th, and a plenary meeting of the Drafting Committee will be held on the 9th to make assumptions.

Preliminary Drafting: The constitution draft research procedure stipulates that the first week, February 23 to March 2, will discuss the territory, groups, sovereignty, and flag colors; the second week, March 2 to March 9, will discuss the issue of people's rights; the third week, March 9 to March 16, will discuss the issue of people's obligations; the fourth week, March 16 to March 23, will discuss the issue of the National Assembly; the fifth week, March 23 to March 23, will discuss the issue of the balance of power between the central and local governments; the sixth week, March 29 to April 5, will discuss the issue of the central government system; the seventh week, April 5 to April 13, will continue; the eighth week, April 13 to April 20, will discuss the issue of the provincial system; the ninth week, April 20 to April 27, will discuss the issue of the county system; the tenth week, April 27 to May 4, will discuss the issue of the right to interpret the constitution and sanctions for violations of the constitution; the eleventh week, May 11 to May 18, will discuss the issue of the exercise of the four powers, the issue of people's livelihood, and the issue of national education; the twelfth week, May 18 to May 25, will discuss the issue of the military system and the issue of national accounting. Preliminary work must be completed by May 25. Afterwards, the assumed items will be reconsidered based on the opinions of all parties and the people.

Presidential Issue: At this point, the reporter asked Mr. Wu for his opinion on the issue of the head of state. Mr. Wu said that he advocates the presidential system. The reporter also asked, "In your opinion, can a military person be the head of state?" Mr. Wu replied, "All people in the Republic of China, whether military or non-military, are equal. Anyone who is respected by the people can take office and cannot be restricted. Don't you hear of the late President Washington of the United States and President Hindenburg of Germany?" At this point, the reporter took his leave.

Ancient Relics Transported from the South Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 103

A Total of 1,054 Boxes

Stored at the Former Site of Renji Hospital

The ancient relics from the Forbidden City in Peiping left Peiping on the 7th of last month and arrived in Pukou on the 9th. Because the central government had not decided on the storage location, they were stranded in Pukou for more than two weeks. They were shipped from Pukou on the 3rd of this month due to the central government deciding to store them in Shanghai. The 1,054 boxes of ancient relics stored in Shanghai arrived in Shanghai at noon yesterday and were transported by automobile to the former site of Renji Hospital at No. 26 Tiantang Street for storage. The details are recorded below:

Arrival in Shanghai 104

The Jiangjing ship loaded the ancient relics in Pukou on the third day and crossed the river to Xiaguan to decide where to store them. The cases of previous dynasties were transported ashore and are now placed in the auditorium of the Executive Yuan. The rest were loaded on the Jiangjing and sailed directly to Shanghai. The Jiangjing entered the port at Shangshi yesterday morning. At 12:00 noon, the ship docked at Jinliyuan Wharf. Soon after, Li Zongtong, Secretary-General of the Museum, inspected and took over. At 1:00 PM, four Mautai foreign company trucks and workers were hired to transport the relics to the sixth floor of the cement building at the former site of Renji Hospital for storage.

Ancient Relics Transported to Shanghai 105

Yesterday, the reporter asked Wu Ying, the secret construction officer who accompanied the ancient relics to Shanghai, about the ancient relics transported to Shanghai. According to him, the total number of boxes transported to Shanghai was 1,056, including books, including the Complete Library of the Four Treasuries, and calligraphy and paintings, including Wang Xizhi's "Clear Weather After Snowfall", which is one of the three rare treasures. The rest are bronze wares, including scattered-character plates and jade wares, and miscellaneous items. The number of boxes transported to Beijing was not limited to this number. However, a department case has been preserved by the Executive Yuan yesterday, so there are only 1,054 boxes. The second batch of ancient relics in Peiping will also be transported to the south. However, we must wait for the empty cars returned from Pukou to go and transport them. In the future, they will probably still have to be transported to Shanghai for storage.

Wharf Protection 106

After the ship arrived in port, the capital's original constitutional soldiers, a company with machine guns, escorted the ship to Shanghai. However, when they arrived at the wharf, the Public Security Bureau dispatched Captain Lu Ying of the Detective Team and Inspector Zhang Zhishan, the Water Patrol Team, etc. to go to the waterway for guard protection. The surprise preparedness headquarters and the French Concession authorities also sent detectives to assist in maintaining order and set up temporary posts at the wharf, which was very strict.

A Glimpse of the Warehouse 107

The reporter visited the temporary warehouse at the former site of Renji Hospital in the afternoon. At that time, half of the ancient relics had been moved. The gate of the house was guarded by Vietnamese guards. Each automobile was jointly protected by a staff member of the Forbidden City and a member of the detective team. Although the surroundings were surrounded by iron cabinets and glass windows, there was fear of leakage. Iron wire mesh was temporarily installed by carpenters. The ancient relics arrived yesterday only reached the third and second floors, and the fourth floor was still empty. Each box of ancient relics was numbered and marked with the word "Wu," which means books. The more valuable items were packed in the original wooden boxes, and the less valuable ones were packed in ordinary large wooden boxes, such as those used to pack cigarettes. Although the house in front of the house was the Renji Hospital, Renji was also leasing it. It is said that the original house belonged to a foreign merchant.

Escort Returning 108

After the constitutional soldiers who escorted the ship to Shanghai yesterday arrived in Shanghai, they were taken over by the local military. Therefore, Secretary-General Li Zongtong ordered them to go to the South Railway Station and take a train back to Beijing last night. As for Secretary Wu Ying, who led eight combatants to Shanghai, was still in the process of sorting things out yesterday. In about two or three days, he would return to Beijing together with Chen Xian, Zhu Zongliang, Zhai Zonghan, and Wang Jinliang, the transport personnel dispatched by the Executive Yuan, and then go to Peiping to take care of the south transport of the second batch of ancient relics. From left to right: Mr. Li Zongtong and Mr. Wu Ying, personnel escorting ancient relics to Shanghai (photographed by Huadong News Agency)

Li Zongtong Speaks 109

The reporter met Li Zongtong, Secretary-General of the Palace Museum of Ancient Relics in Peiping, in the warehouse on Tiantang Street. At that time, Wen Hong'en, Director of the Public Security Bureau, was also at the French Concession Police Station. Section Chief (French) was contacting Mr. Li about the night protection. The French police agreed to dispatch five people to jointly protect the site with five detectives from the Public Security Bureau. According to Mr. Li, the ancient relics have now been transported, but this number is only one-fifth of the total. In the future, they will continue to be transported to the south one after another. We are now hiring Mautai freight trucks. At this rate, it will definitely not be finished by tomorrow. Therefore, ten more trucks were hired in the afternoon. Even so, it will not be completed until 8:00 PM in the evening. The warehouse rent is 3,750 taels per month, and the contract is for half a year. In the past, it was decided not to store it in Shanghai anymore, so there was a refund of 2,000 taels. Now that we have leased it, we will continue to do so. Regarding the security of the warehouse, I am negotiating with Director Wen, but it has not yet been decided. In general, there will be a random inspection of the ancient relics once every period. I will complete the Shanghai affairs and then go to Beijing to report. As for the date of the south transport of the second batch and the storage location, it is difficult to predict. There is still space in the Shanghai house now. In general, the ones coming south in the future will still be stored in Shanghai.

Shanghai Fishery Association Held Its Inaugural Meeting Yesterday 110

Party and Government Agencies Sent Representatives to Give Instructions

Central News Agency reports: The Shanghai Fishery Association, which has been in preparation for many years, held its inaugural meeting at Dunhe Public Office, No. Lujiazhai Lane, Xiaodongmen yesterday. A total of more than 90 representatives of fishermen and fish merchants attended, as well as more than 100 guests, including Lu Yinchu, representative of the Municipal Party Committee, Wang Defa, representative of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Luo Yu, representative of the Jiangzhe Fisheries Administration Bureau, and other guests. At 10:00 AM, the bell rang to open the meeting. According to the agenda, they began to discuss proposals and elect directors and supervisors. After lunch, the ballots were counted again. It was not until 4:00 PM in the afternoon that the election results were announced. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Ceremony Order 111

1. Ring the bell to open the meeting. 2. All stand at attention. 3. Bow three times to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister. 4. The chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will. 5. Silence. 6. The chairman reports on the purpose of the meeting. 7. The preparatory committee reports on the preparation process. 8. Party and government representatives give instructions. 9. Guests speak. 10. Discuss the association's charter. 11. Discuss proposals. 12. Elect directors and supervisors. 13. Report the election results. All the staff at the meeting were tentatively nominated in advance by the preparatory committee. The presidium consisted of seven people: Zhang Shenzhi, Fang Jiaobo, Dai Yongting, Wu Zhenxin, Zhu Bao, Wu Xintai, Ge Liquan, and several people as master of ceremonies, recorders, and receptionists.

Various Reports 112

After performing the ceremony as required, Chairman Fang Jiaobo first reported on the purpose of the meeting, saying roughly that the city's fishermen and fish merchants have never had a unified organization. This time, in order to seek the welfare of the fishermen and fish merchants themselves, we have brought together fishermen, fish shops, and store merchants from all over the city to organize the City Fishery Association, which is of great significance, and so on. Then, Zhang Shenzhi, a member of the preparatory committee, reported on the preparation process, saying roughly that the city's fishermen and fish merchants initiated the organization of the City Fishery Association this time based on the Central Fishery Association Law, and appointed me and others to serve as members of the preparatory committee to handle all preparation matters. Because the procedures were more complicated, it has been a year since the preparation began. We have now solicited more than a thousand members and have reported to the party and government agencies for filing. Today, we are holding a formal inaugural meeting, and all previous preparations have come to an end, he said.

Abstract of Instructions 113

Lu Yinchu, representative of the Municipal Party Committee, gave instructions, saying roughly that China has always been an agricultural country, and fisheries are also an important part. Therefore, we should attach importance to fisheries. Today, the City Fishery Association is established in the city, and directors and supervisors will be elected. In the future, the relationship between all members and directors and supervisors should be close, so that they can exchange ideas, alleviate their own pain, and improve their own careers. Then, Wang Defa, representative of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, gave instructions, saying roughly that the length of China's coastline is much longer than that of Japan, but China's fishery market has been encroached upon by Japanese merchants. This is due to the backwardness of China's fishery technology. Therefore, in the future, under a unified organization, we should strive to improve China's fisheries so that hate goods cannot appear in China's fishery market. Next, Luo Zibao, representative of the Fisheries Bureau, gave instructions, saying roughly that the mission undertaken by the establishment of the City Fishery Association today is of great significance. Fisheries are a major production industry, and Shanghai is the center of the national production industry. Therefore, in the future, all our fishermen and fish merchants should seek the improvement of fisheries for the benefit of the entire nation. There were also speeches by Feng Limin, Principal of Wusong Fisheries School, and Wang Wentai, Director of Jiangsu Fisheries Experimental Farm, and others. The speeches were lengthy and are omitted here.

Eight Important Cases 114

1. Representative Xu Yifei proposed that attention should be paid to the Fishery Improvement Association, which will have similar fishery taxes. We must oppose the case. It was resolved and submitted to the board of directors. 2. Representative Xu Yifei proposed that the conference strictly prohibit the sale of fresh fish from Japanese fishing boats, regardless of national disgrace, or the loading of Japanese fish on Chinese sailboats at the mouth of Wusong, pretending to be Chinese fishing boat goods and selling them in Shanghai. It was resolved and submitted to the board of directors. 3. Representative Shen Mingzhe proposed that Japan is invading Jehol and the national crisis is deepening. We should initiate the raising of funds for the [Shanghai Fishery No.] airplane to resist the violent Japan. It was resolved and submitted to the board of directors to stipulate fundraising measures. 4. The River Fresh Fish Industry proposed that the river fresh fish industry has been suffering from extortion by military police and local hooligans along the way for many years, and the pain is great. Measures should be taken to provide relief. It was resolved and submitted to the board of directors, and truthfully reported to the party and government authorities for strict ban. 5. The Preparatory Committee proposed that the association's funds should be determined. It was resolved that the board of directors should negotiate and handle the matter. 6. The Preparatory Committee proposed that the government should allocate the offshore fishing merchant's ocean protection business to the association for handling, and recover the Fufu and Liangyu fishing boats. It was resolved and submitted to the board of directors for handling. 7. Representative Yu Chuhu proposed that the conference should ask the government to stop the extortion of salt fish transportation by anti-smuggling camps. It was resolved and passed. 8. Representative Yu Chuhu et al. proposed that the sales of Japanese fish by fishing merchants should be strictly controlled to benefit the national fishery. It was resolved and handled in conjunction with the second case.

Association Charter Content 115

The charter consists of seven chapters and thirty-six articles: Chapter 1 General Provisions, Chapter 2 Association Affairs, Chapter 3 Membership, Chapter 4 Organization, Chapter 5 Meetings, Chapter 6 Funds, Chapter 7 Supplementary Provisions.

Wang Delin's Entry into Russia: 117

Detailed Account of Anti-Japanese Situation

It is now known that Liang Yinshan, a special envoy from a certain military organization in Beiping, has returned to China after General Commander Wang Delin of the Jilin National Salvation Army retreated into Russian territory last month due to exhaustion of ammunition and lack of reinforcements. His report on Wang Delin's retreat into Russia is extremely detailed. The original text of his report is as follows (excerpted above): I was dispatched from Beiping on January 27th of this year and arrived in Qingdao on the 31st. On February 2nd, I took a boat to Dalian, and the next day, I arrived in Harbin. On the 5th, I arrived in Yimianpo and was slightly ill for several days. On the night of the 9th, I arrived at Bazhan (i.e., Maqiao River). On the 12th, I arrived at Suifenhe to investigate everything. I started my return journey on the 14th and returned to Beiping on the 21st. Now, I will list the situation at the front line as follows: General Commander Wang Delin was suddenly subjected to pressure and engaged in a fierce battle with the enemy at Wanlonggou, which belongs to the jurisdiction of Chezi County. The Japanese invaders suffered heavy casualties. It is rumored that the enemy side seized the bodies of officers and soldiers who died in battle, amounting to seventeen sleighs. Each sleigh could hold at least thirty bodies, so the number of deaths is obvious. Our army was attacked from above and below by the enemy's tanks and airplanes. With ammunition exhausted and no reinforcements, we had to retreat south to Dongning. We continued to resist at places such as Daxiao Wushaogou and Foyegou, holding on with flesh and blood. However, the snow in the mountains was several feet deep, and there was no suitable way out. After a fierce battle, the entire army carefully considered the advantages and disadvantages. The masses gathered and decided to force General Commander Wang to temporarily enter Russian territory in order to remove the target of the violent Japanese and to preserve our strength. In this environment, General Commander Wang led a small number of trusted cavalry and infantry units, as well as the families of generals and refugees, and retreated into the Shuangchengpu area of Russia on January 15th. Before departing, General Commander Wang emphasized local security and ordered Deputy Commander Kong Xianrong to lead strong troops to resist at the rear. Therefore, the people and merchants of Dongning did not suffer any losses. After General Commander Wang completely withdrew from the country, Deputy Commander Kong also entered Russia. Currently, all the troops in the Yanji and Dunhua areas are under the authority of Deputy Commander Wu Yicheng, who is acting as the commander-in-chief. Deputy Commander Wu and Staff Officer Li led the majority of the troops directly to Suifen Dadianzi, Huapidianzi, Nanbeichengzigou, and Daxiao Putaogou, through Zhuanjiaolou, taking the road through Chengzicun, Tongzigou, and reaching Songshuling, stationed at Nanhutou, in order to cut off the Japanese army's road from Dunhua to Mian. They are currently reorganizing their troops and actively planning a counterattack, as well as urgently destroying the Yan-Hui and Mudanjiang bank's Middle Eastern Railway tracks. Their momentum is more active than before. After this major stimulation, the soldiers' determination to kill the enemy and recover the land is even stronger. Those in the Hunchun and Wangqing areas are under the command of Deputy Commander Wang Yuzhen. The situation of the battle is unknown. It is also heard that Zhao Rongxian, the liaison officer sent by the rear, and Gao, the adjutant sent by Supervisor Wan to inspect the troops, have already gone to Russia with General Commander Wang. The whereabouts of other liaison officers, such as Liu Yichen, are still unknown. The various armies led by War Supervisor Zhang Yuting and Zheng Xing are still holding strategic locations in Muleng Liangzihe and Baicaogou, waiting for an opportunity to move. This is all the real situation.

Robbers on Weituoma Road Resist Arrest and Open Fire 120

Exchanging More Than Twenty Rounds of Gunfire

All Four Robbers Arrested, One Wounded

- Stray Bullet Wounds Passerby Liu Guoxun -

Yesterday at around 5 PM, Li Pengfei, Detective No. 98 of the Yulin Road Police Station, received a tip that robbers would be passing through the intersection of Longjiang Road and Weituoma Road to commit robbery. After receiving the report, Li reported to the chief, who dispatched the entire squad of detectives to arrest them. As they approached Weituoma Road, four men suddenly appeared on the side of the road, acting suspiciously. Li knew they were not good people and prepared to go forward to search them. Unexpectedly, the robbers noticed them and, as the detectives attempted to arrest them, the robbers drew their guns and opened fire on the detectives. The detectives returned fire, and a fierce battle ensued. Bullets flew thick and fast, and they exchanged fire for about twenty rounds. One of the robbers was shot down first. When the remaining robbers saw this, they were terrified and were captured by the detectives in one fell swoop. Two handguns were confiscated and taken to the police station for safekeeping. The wounded robber was sent to the Municipal Council Hospital. It is reported that the robber's name is Zheng Dengcai, 28 years old, and he was shot seven times in the head, waist, right leg, right knee, left arm, left leg, and back. His injuries are quite serious. During the battle between the detectives and the robbers, a passerby was wounded by a stray bullet. The bullet passed through his left chest. The detectives sent him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, his injuries were minor and he is not in danger. It is also learned that the person's name is Liu Guoxun, 30 years old, from Funing, and he works as a salesman for the Jiuli Oil Company on Meizhou Road. He lives inside the No. 5 gate of the Shenxin Yarn Factory's workers' quarters on Meizhou Road.

Establishment of the Shanghai Expo Exhibitors Association 121

Election of Cai Yuanpei and Fifteen Others as Directors - Establishment of Four Working Groups, Determination of Directors and Deputy Directors

Exhibition Closing Last Night, Announcement of Return of Exhibits

After the central government stopped participating in the Chicago Expo, the exhibitors decided to form their own association to participate in the U.S. The Exhibitors Association was officially established yesterday, and Cai Yuanpei and fifteen others were elected as directors, and He Bingxian and eight others were elected as directors and deputy directors of various groups. The exhibition closed at 7 PM last night, and a newspaper announcement has been made today that the exhibits will be returned starting tomorrow. The Review Committee has also decided to issue certificates of merit to qualified exhibits to encourage them. The details are recorded below:

Exhibitors Association Officially Established 122

Yesterday at 3 PM, the exhibitors convened a general meeting at the exhibition site to formally establish the Exhibitors Association. More than 20 exhibitors, including Zhou Guanhong and Cao Jinhui, attended. Zhou Guanhong was elected as chairman, and Dong Guangying was the recorder. After the chairman's report, the association's charter and the regulations of the Economic Committee were discussed. They were revised and approved item by item. Then, directors and directors and deputy directors of various groups were elected, and the basic exhibits for participating in the Chicago Expo were determined to be: (1) jade; (2) lacquerware; (3) porcelain; (4) tea; (5) embroidery; (6) carpets; (7) art; (8) ramie cloth; (9) pottery; (10) silk; (11) printing; (12) carving.

Charter Passed, Economic Committee Established 123

The association passed a charter with a total of twenty-one articles, stipulating that fifteen directors should be elected by the general meeting of members to represent the association in executing all association affairs. For the convenience of administration, four groups were established: (1) General Affairs, (2) Custody, (3) Publicity, and (4) Social Affairs, to perform their respective duties. At the same time, the regulations of the Economic Committee were passed, with one director and one deputy director in charge of planning and managing the funds for participating in the Chicago Expo and auditing the association's budget and final accounts. The board of directors is scheduled to meet every Wednesday, and it is planned to invite leaders from all walks of life as sponsors and submit a request to the Ministry of Industry for record-keeping.

Cai Yuanpei and Others Elected as Directors 124

In accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the association's charter, Cai Yuanpei, Wang Xiaolai, Ye Gongchuo, Zhang Xianglin, Miao Zhongxiu, Xu Xinliu, Qian Xinzhi, Lin Kanghou, He Bingxian, Cai Wuji, Zhao Jinqing, Zhou Guanhong, Cao Jinhui, Dong Kunfan, and Wu Guangzhi were elected as fifteen directors. In accordance with Article 6 of the charter, the directors of each group were determined as follows: (1) General Affairs Group: Director Cao Jinhui, Deputy Director Zhou Guanhong; (2) Custody Group: Director Miao Zhongxiu, Deputy Director Zhang Zhidi; (3) Publicity Group: Director He Bingxian, Deputy Director Mo Keming; (4) Social Affairs Group: Director Zhang Xianglin, Deputy Director Shao Dehui.

Exhibition Closes, Exhibits Returned 125

Yesterday was the last day of the exhibit exhibition. More than 7,000 people attended. Wu De, the German consul in Shanghai, attended and ordered a large number of porcelain. The exhibition was declared closed at 7 PM. All exhibits have been notified by Xu Baohua, director of the General Affairs Section, to the various exhibitors to bring their receipts to the association on Bailinan Road from tomorrow until the 11th, from 9 AM to 12 PM and from 2 PM to 5 PM every day to retrieve their exhibits. Exhibits from other locations will be shipped back after the 11th and will be announced in the newspaper today. The Review Committee has also decided to issue certificates to all qualified exhibits, regardless of grade, to encourage them.

Poisonous Snake Den Discovered in Qibao Town, Western Shanghai 126

A Total of Forty to Fifty Snakes

The Largest is More Than Five Feet Long

In Qibao Town, southwest of the Dasi Street in western Shanghai, there is a house inhabited by the Tang family. The northwest side of the house is surrounded by trees, vegetables, and other plants. Now that spring has arrived, they plan to turn over the garden soil and plant vegetables. The day before yesterday, while digging up dead trees and moving broken tiles, they suddenly discovered more than ten snakes, commonly known as "red-banded krait" and "ash viper". Yesterday, they saw eight or nine more. Today, as the moving and digging were nearing completion, they discovered a large pile of these snakes again, counting more than twenty. The largest was more than five feet long, and the smallest was more than one foot long. Because it was not yet the Jingzhe (Awakening of Insects) solar term, they were shaped like dead creatures but wriggling. The Tang family quickly killed them with iron hoes and burned them to prevent them from leaving poison. This matter spread throughout the town and was regarded as a strange event.

The Butcher Prepares to Slaughter

The Detective Steps Forward to Stop Him

Salary Reduction Dispute at the Grains Exchange 128

Between Seventy and Ninety Percent

Due to poor business, the Shanghai Grains, Oil, and Cake Exchange has been paying its employees only seventy percent of their original salaries since January of last year, causing dissatisfaction among the employees. They all believed that the exchange had not yet suffered losses and should not reduce salaries. Therefore, they requested several times without success and petitioned various party and government agencies for mediation. The Social Bureau recently summoned representatives from both labor and management for mediation, but the management claimed that due to sluggish business, paying seventy percent of the salary was a last resort. However, the labor side argued that although business had declined last year, there was still a surplus, and salaries should not be discounted. The two sides remained deadlocked and the issue was not resolved. It is now learned that after mediation by someone, the exchange's board of directors discussed the salaries of the employees again and again and decided to pay eighty-five percent of the original salaries. The salaries will be restored to their original levels after the business recovers. It is heard that some people on the employee side also made some concessions and requested to receive ninety percent of the salary as a temporary measure. If the business is booming, the deducted salaries will be compensated in full. After the mediator's explanation, the matter should be resolved soon.

Due to the Prevalence of Smallpox

Effective from March 7th

Wu Liande, the director of the Seaport Quarantine Administration, has found that there have been recent cases of smallpox in Hong Kong. Here is the original notice: Seaport Quarantine Administration Notice No. 31, Notice: It has been found that there is a smallpox epidemic in Hong Kong. This office has set March 7th as the date to declare the port to be a port with an epidemic. All ships arriving in Shanghai from that port will be subject to inspection by quarantine officials upon arrival in Shanghai. Passengers, crew members, and sailors will be inspected without exception. No one is allowed to disembark without permission until the office has issued a traffic permit. The Zhengtai Factory Disaster has been Reported to the Social Bureau 131

A Compensation of 300 Yuan for Each Deceased Worker

Seventy-One of the Eighty-One Families Have Already Received It

Since the disastrous incident at the Shanghai Zhengtai Rubber Factory, the factory has been handling the aftermath. Yesterday, they also submitted a report to the Social Bureau on the circumstances of the disaster for record-keeping. The original report is as follows: Reporting on the circumstances of the disastrous accident at our factory, as well as the handling of the aftermath, requesting review and approval, etc. In response to Order No. Shezi 9121, within, etc. (excerpted), This order, etc. In response, we found that our factory suffered an unfortunate accident at 9:30 AM on the 21st of last month. We were about to investigate and report in accordance with the Factory Law, but due to the extraordinary nature of the incident and the magnitude of the disaster, the number of deaths and injuries was not easy to investigate for a while, resulting in a delay. The reason for the cylinder explosion that day was that the electrical wire behind the steam cylinder in the southern part of our factory short-circuited, igniting the paint oil drums nearby. The oil was flammable, so after the fire started, all ten or so drums of paint oil burned at the same time. The temperature rose sharply, and the four boilers connected to the paint oil, including one large and one small, were filled with air. Affected by the extremely high temperature outside, the air pressure increased and exploded one after another. The entire factory collapsed, and the sound of the explosions shook the sky. It was unbearable to witness. Seventy-five female workers and six male workers died in the disaster, a total of eighty-one people. Three male workers and fifteen female workers are still being treated in the hospital, a total of eighteen people. The bodies of all eighty-one deceased male and female workers have been examined by the court and sent to the Pushan Villa for burial. Our factory deeply mourns the deceased workers and has purchased coffins, silk bedding, and silk floss for the burial. The coffins were temporarily placed in the hospital and then transported to Shanghai by the Beijing-Shanghai train and temporarily placed in the Zhonghua Hotel on Jielu Road. Li then went around looking for a buyer. On the 27th of last month, Li Arong entrusted Li Erda of Changzhou to sell her, and Li Erda led his accomplice, Shen Xiaosan of Jiangbei, to pretend to be the woman's husband in order to facilitate the sale. After several days of running around, a man named Wang Baobao wanted to buy the woman. Li and others then invited Wang and Wang's friend, Yang Axin, to the Zhonghua Hotel to negotiate. Shen Xiaosan, the woman's fake husband, asked for 400 yuan. Unexpectedly, the matter was heard by detectives Wang Xichang and Yang Xinzheng of the Jingansi Road Police Station, who rushed to the hotel to arrest them the day before yesterday. Li Erda and Shen Xiaosan were arrested on the spot, but Li Arong had already escaped in advance. The detectives then escorted the two traffickers and Chen Er, who had been abducted repeatedly, to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. Although Chen Er is a country girl, she is naturally beautiful. Even in a black cotton jacket and pants, she cannot hide her natural beauty. Those who saw her said that with such beauty, it is no wonder that she was repeatedly lured by traitors while alone outside. At that time, the police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that the defendants had abducted a woman from a good family, sold her into prostitution, and then abducted her again for sale, which was a heinous crime, and requested that they be severely punished. After the woman detailed the circumstances of the abduction, Judge Wu Tingqi questioned the two defendants, Li Erda and Shen Xiaosan, and the witness, Wang Baobao, one by one, and ordered the defendants to be detained. The woman was temporarily sent to the Jiliang Institute for further interrogation at a later date.

The Jiangyin Guild Hall has purchased four mu of land in Datang to build a public cemetery for the workers who died in the disaster to comfort their souls. The factory's board of directors has also repeatedly discussed the issue of compensation for the families of the deceased workers and has decided to provide a compensation of 300 yuan per family. Seventy-one families have already come to the factory to collect it, and the rest will be paid as soon as they collect it. The factory will continue to pay the male workers who escaped the disaster their original salaries to maintain their livelihoods. Those who wish to return to their hometowns will be given travel expenses. After the factory's machinery is repaired, they will be notified to return to work. The female workers who escaped the disaster will be transferred to the factory's second factory as soon as possible to avoid unemployment. All of the above is a general overview of the efforts made by our factory to handle the aftermath. Rubber manufacturing has been suffering from the encroachment of Japanese goods for years, and business has plummeted. Since the January 28th Incident last year, the damage has been even greater. All businesses in this industry are on the verge of collapse. Our factory suffered a major disaster this time, making it even more difficult to sustain itself. However, we believe that the workers sacrificed their lives in the line of duty, which is very regrettable. Therefore, we have been working hard to handle the aftermath and compensation matters, hoping to live up to our conscience. In accordance with the order, we have submitted a report on the disaster and the handling of the aftermath. We hope that you will review and approve it for the benefit of the public. Respectfully submitted to Wu, Director of the Shanghai Social Bureau.

Ministry of Industry Instructs Municipal Chambers of Commerce to Promote Industrial Standardization 138

Regulations on Methods of Recording Information on Goods

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce received Instruction No. 6181 from the Ministry of Industry, stating that the National Bureau of Weights and Measures reported that industrial standardization is closely related to the unification of weights and measures. Taking the item of recording quantities on goods as an example, many countries have explicit legal provisions, and our country has also adopted some, but they are not very common, and they mostly use various complex weights and measures of other countries or old systems, which have no prospect of unification and cause many obstacles. Now, three preliminary measures are drafted as follows: (1) For goods that are easy to record quantities, the quantity should be clearly recorded on the original product or its packaging when leaving the factory, such as the length and width of a piece of cloth. (2) The quantity marked on the goods shall not exceed the actual quantity. For example, if a box of biscuits actually weighs one catty, it shall not be marked as more than one catty on the box. (3) The measurement of goods shall be based on the new system of weights and measures and shall not misuse the old system or foreign weights and measures. The above-mentioned three preliminary measures, if implemented nationwide, will be of some benefit to the unification of weights and measures. Whether they are feasible, it is appropriate to submit a document for review and compliance. If approved, it is proposed to issue a notice to all chambers of commerce and trade associations across the country to comply accordingly.

Huai River Advancement Association Established Yesterday 140

Gu Zhuxuan and others Elected as Executive Committee Members

The Jiangsu Huai River Guidance Association held its inaugural meeting at 3:00 p.m. yesterday at the Zhabei Charity Association on Datong Road, Zhabei. 106 members attended, and Mao Xiaxuan, a representative from the Municipal Party Department, attended and participated. After performing the formalities, Cheng Xiechun was publicly elected as the chairman. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the association, followed by the election of 21 executive committee members. The elected members were Gu Zhuxuan, Cheng Xiechun, Shan Meishu, Ji Longtu, Yang Shaopeng, Wang Yunzhi, Chen Bomeng, Zhang Mumin, Guo Jifen, Hu Xianbai, Wu Yibai, Zhu Dexuan, Zhou Ang, Ling Yuqing, Wang Xiufu, Chen Chaobi, etc. Then, the articles of association were adopted, and the meeting was adjourned. The articles of association of the association are recorded as follows: Article 1: This association is named the Jiangsu Huai River Guidance Advancement Association. Article 2: The purpose of this association is to study the relationship between the Huai River and Jiangsu, the route of guidance and governance, its procedures, and to contribute to the authorities to assist in the progress. Article 3: The association's office is attached to the Shanghai Zhabei Jianghuai Fellow Townsmen Association office (temporarily located at No. 309, Yingchunfang, Hubei Road). Article 4: Any Jiangsu people who agree with the purpose of the association and volunteer to join the association, upon the introduction of two members and the approval of the executive committee member, shall become a member of the association. Article 5: This association shall have 21 executive committee members and 9 alternate executive committee members to form a committee as the executive organ, which shall be elected by the general meeting, and those with the most votes shall be elected. Article 6: This association shall have 5 standing committee members elected from the executive committee members to form a standing committee to carry out daily affairs. Article 7: This association shall have five groups: general affairs, investigation, research, publicity, and compilation. The executive committee members of each group shall be hired by the members themselves, and each group shall have a director and a deputy director. The detailed rules shall be formulated separately. Article 8: The duties of each group of this association are as follows: (1) The general affairs group shall be in charge of documents, accounting, public relations, general affairs, and matters not belonging to other groups. (2) The investigation group shall be in charge of researching water conservancy and conducting on-site surveys. (3) The research group shall be in charge of studying the advantages and disadvantages of water management and the planning and construction procedures. (4) The publicity group shall be in charge of publicizing the purpose of the association and the progress procedures. (5) The compilation group shall be in charge of compiling books, publications, and writing manuscripts. Article 9: The investigation, research, and compilation groups of this association may propose to the executive committee of this association to hire engineers and technicians with specialized knowledge and experience in water conservancy. Article 10: The executive committee members may be re-elected annually. The method of re-election shall be that the association shall hold a general meeting of members once a year. If there are special matters, the standing committee members shall convene a temporary meeting. Article 11: The executive committee of this association shall meet once a month. The meetings of each group shall be convened by the directors of each group. Article 12: The membership fee of this association shall be borne by the members, each person 2 yuan per year, which shall be paid at the general meeting. Article 13: The articles of association of this association shall be implemented after being approved by the general meeting. Article 14: Matters not covered in these articles of association shall be decided and amended by the general meeting of members.

Overview of War Damage to the Law School 142

Total Loss Exceeds 430,000 Yuan

The Shanghai Law School in Jiangwan was bombed by the violent Japanese army during the January 28th Shanghai Incident. The losses suffered during the national crisis have been ascertained and compiled into [Overview of Losses of Shanghai Law School in the National Crisis]. The construction of buildings, equipment, and books totaled 303,580 yuan. The private losses [such as faculty, staff, and students] of bedding, luggage, books, works, daily necessities, etc., totaled 130,710 yuan. Ten photos of the destroyed school buildings, dormitories, auditoriums, and classrooms were taken and explained. The school was founded in the summer of 1926, initially named Shanghai Law University, renting private houses on Pubo Road in the French Concession as lecture halls. Zhang Binglin and Dong Kang served as presidents and vice presidents, respectively. Before long, Zhang resigned and organized a board of directors in accordance with the law, electing Chu Fucheng as chairman, and Dong Kang and Pan Dadao as vice chairmen. In 1927, Pan was assassinated, and Dong also resigned. Qian Yongming was re-elected as chairman, and Chu as president, and Shen Junru as dean of academic affairs, and continued to run the school, striving for improvement. The number of students increased, and the school buildings were insufficient. Therefore, in August 1928, the school moved to Jiangwan Road in Zhabei, with a total area of 15 mu. The classroom dormitory archway was completed in 1929 and could accommodate 1,500 people. The lecture halls and dormitories were divided into 47 rooms and could accommodate 300 people. In 1930, in accordance with the instructions of the Ministry of Education, the school was renamed Shanghai Private Law School. In the winter of that year, it was approved for registration. In the spring of 1931, a large auditorium was added. The above situation was carefully managed over the years, and the total amount of school funds reached 400,000 yuan. Unfortunately, it was destroyed by the violent Japanese army on January 28th, and everything was reduced to ashes. The School had organized a restoration committee and plans to raise 100,000 yuan. It is currently engaged in repairs. Once the school buildings are repaired, all the students of the school can move back to Jiangwan Road from Yaozhu Road.

Marriage Problem 145

Inquiry from Ms. Luo Shuqing

I am eighteen years old this year and grew up in an old-fashioned family. I only studied in a private school for one year. My parents are very conservative and afraid that I will be influenced by new trends, so they do not allow me to go to school. All day long, I am confined to my deep and closed cage. Reading the newspaper is how I study.

The reader’s answers to questions all make me admire them to the point of prostration. I also ask you to give me guidance on the difficult problem I sigh about every day. When I was twelve years old, my parents made a match for me with the son of a wealthy man in a deep rural area. At that time, I was ignorant and of course did not object. Later, as my knowledge gradually improved, I realized that marriage was my biggest problem. I paid attention to inquiring about everything about my fiancé and also met him. He is not yet twenty years old and is already a drunkard, drinking alcohol before every meal. He is still asking an eight-legged essay teacher to teach him the Classic of Poetry and ancient texts at home. Can that be useful? I live in the city and have been slightly influenced by newspapers and magazines. Frankly speaking, I am unwilling to marry someone who is neither a farmer nor a worker and who sits and eats up his ancestors’ inheritance. I would rather die! There is a man next door to me who is about the same age as me. Although his situation is humble, he can be said to have a noble personality. I have been paying attention to him for more than a year, and all his habits are just like my ideals. We sometimes meet, and we are both very shy. There is no need to say that we admire each other. One day, I received a letter without a head or tail. I guess it was written by him. Since then, we have corresponded frequently. I have also had a few dangerous encounters where I talked to him in the park, and we are even more in harmony. It is hateful that although I want to deny this purely despotic marriage contract and break away from this unproductive and incompatible fiancé, I cannot express my private thoughts to my parents in such a corrupt family. It is impossible for them to grant my wishes. My future is extremely hopeless. I heard that my husband’s family will soon be looking for a date to marry me, which is tantamount to my death date approaching. Mr. Chang said that suicide is absolutely not allowed. If I marry into a remote rural town, I will be extorting blood and sweat from a wealthy man, and I will break off my friendship with my friends. I feel that life is worse than death. Only Mr. Mist Haina Zhen, please show me the answer. Answer: The handwriting of the lady’s letter is beautiful and the writing is clear and coherent. It is naturally impossible to have this achievement after studying in a private school for one year. Rather, it is the result of the lady having a remarkable talent and the virtue of self-study. Admirable, admirable! However, it is distressing to see such a determined and eager-to-learn woman being bound by an old-fashioned family and suffering from unfree marriage, and it is even hateful that I have no power to actively help the lady! For the sake of the lady... the first step is to try to persuade your father and mother to ask them to let you come out to study... But for the time being, you must not express your intention to refuse marriage, just say that you will talk about it after you return from studying... If they agree to your request, then there will be a way for the second step. After you arrive in Shanghai, study hard for a year, or work a little harder and help your lover study. You must not get married immediately or have further relations with him; because you do not know how to prevent childbirth, if other results occur, then not only will you have no joy to enjoy in the future, but you will also suffer. After a year, you will both have a little foundation outside, and then write a letter to tell them the reason why you cannot be engaged to the wealthy man's son, and ask them to forgive you. Perhaps they will not be stubborn, otherwise, if you really love each other, then you should leave your family and work in the factory, live independently, and help each other. Although it is a little hard in terms of material things, you can get some compensation in spirit. The marriage problem is one of the modern social problems. If the social problem is not fundamentally solved, this problem will not be solved satisfactorily. The opinions we offer are also a last resort, and it depends on the lady's efforts!

Ding Shaoxian Commits Suicide Due to Neglect of Duty 147

Ding Shaoxian, a native of Zhaiqi Town, Hangzhou, is 36 years old this year. He was engaged in the paper business and worked at Kang Dingchang Shop in Zhoupu Town, Nanhui County, Pudong. He has a wife and children at home. Recently, he used the funds in the shop and was dismissed by the manager and came to Shanghai, intending to find another place to live. Unfortunately, he could not find a place. On the evening of the 3rd, he checked into Room 18 of the Huatong Inn, No. 381, Aiduya Road, French Concession, under the assumed name of Ding Yuyu. He stayed until the evening of the 4th. Because he could not find a job, he was stimulated for a while and had a momentary thought. He secretly swallowed raw opium and committed suicide. By yesterday, it was already past noon. The teaboy, Wang Yu, saw that he had not yet gotten up, so at 1:00 p.m., he knocked on the door as usual, asking if the room was needed. He knocked on the door and called for a long time, but there was no response in the room. He knew that something had happened, so he pried open the door and went in to check. Ding had already died in bed, his body was as cold as ice. He immediately reported to the French Police Station, which sent a detective to investigate. A suicide note was found on the deceased, with two letters, one addressed to his younger brother Ding Xiuchang, instructing him to take care of his wife and children, and one entrusted to his teacher, the owner of Kang Dingchang, saying that the funds were lost due to being harmed by others, and he was now forced to commit suicide. The body was sent to the Tongren Foyuantang autopsy site and reported to the court for examination today.
